--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/PlayerModule_contents/ControlModule_contents/VRNavigation.lua ---

--[[
    VRNavigation (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → PlayerModule → ControlModule
    Parent: ControlModule
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:55
]]

--[[
		VRNavigation
--]]

local VRService = game:GetService("VRService")
local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local PathfindingService = game:GetService("PathfindingService")
local ContextActionService = game:GetService("ContextActionService")
local StarterGui = game:GetService("StarterGui")

--local MasterControl = require(script.Parent)
local PathDisplay = nil
local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer

--[[ Constants ]]--
local RECALCULATE_PATH_THRESHOLD = 4
local NO_PATH_THRESHOLD = 12
local MAX_PATHING_DISTANCE = 200
local POINT_REACHED_THRESHOLD = 1
local OFFTRACK_TIME_THRESHOLD = 2
local THUMBSTICK_DEADZONE = 0.22

local ZERO_VECTOR3 = Vector3.new(0,0,0)
local XZ_VECTOR3 = Vector3.new(1,0,1)

--[[ Utility Functions ]]--
local function IsFinite(num)
	return num == num and num ~= 1/0 and num ~= -1/0
end

local function IsFiniteVector3(vec3)
	return IsFinite(vec3.x) and IsFinite(vec3.y) and IsFinite(vec3.z)
end

local movementUpdateEvent = Instance.new("BindableEvent")
movementUpdateEvent.Name = "MovementUpdate"
movementUpdateEvent.Parent = script

coroutine.wrap(function()
	local PathDisplayModule = script.Parent:WaitForChild("PathDisplay")
	if PathDisplayModule then
		PathDisplay = require(PathDisplayModule)
	end
end)()


--[[ The Class ]]--
local BaseCharacterController = require(script.Parent:WaitForChild("BaseCharacterController"))
local VRNavigation = setmetatable({}, BaseCharacterController)
VRNavigation.__index = VRNavigation

function VRNavigation.new(CONTROL_ACTION_PRIORITY)
	local self = setmetatable(BaseCharacterController.new(), VRNavigation)

	self.CONTROL_ACTION_PRIORITY = CONTROL_ACTION_PRIORITY

	self.navigationRequestedConn = nil
	self.heartbeatConn = nil

	self.currentDestination = nil
	self.currentPath = nil
	self.currentPoints = nil
	self.currentPointIdx = 0

	self.expectedTimeToNextPoint = 0
	self.timeReachedLastPoint = tick()
	self.moving = false

	self.isJumpBound = false
	self.moveLatch = false

	self.userCFrameEnabledConn = nil

	return self
end

function VRNavigation:SetLaserPointerMode(mode)
	pcall(function()
		StarterGui:SetCore("VRLaserPointerMode", mode)
	end)
end

function VRNavigation:GetLocalHumanoid()
	local character = LocalPlayer.Character
	if not character then
		return
	end

	for _, child in pairs(character:GetChildren()) do
		if child:IsA("Humanoid") then
			return child
		end
	end
	return nil
end

function VRNavigation:HasBothHandControllers()
	return VRService:GetUserCFrameEnabled(Enum.UserCFrame.RightHand) and VRService:GetUserCFrameEnabled(Enum.UserCFrame.LeftHand)
end

function VRNavigation:HasAnyHandControllers()
	return VRService:GetUserCFrameEnabled(Enum.UserCFrame.RightHand) or VRService:GetUserCFrameEnabled(Enum.UserCFrame.LeftHand)
end

function VRNavigation:IsMobileVR()
	return UserInputService.TouchEnabled
end

function VRNavigation:HasGamepad()
	return UserInputService.GamepadEnabled
end

function VRNavigation:ShouldUseNavigationLaser()
	--Places where we use the navigation laser:
	-- mobile VR with any number of hands tracked
	-- desktop VR with only one hand tracked
	-- desktop VR with no hands and no gamepad (i.e. with Oculus remote?)
	--using an Xbox controller with a desktop VR headset means no laser since the user has a thumbstick.
	--in the future, we should query thumbstick presence with a features API
	if self:IsMobileVR() then
		return true
	else
		if self:HasBothHandControllers() then
			return false
		end
		if not self:HasAnyHandControllers() then
			return not self:HasGamepad()
		end
		return true
	end
end



function VRNavigation:StartFollowingPath(newPath)
	currentPath = newPath
	currentPoints = currentPath:GetPointCoordinates()
	currentPointIdx = 1
	moving = true

	timeReachedLastPoint = tick()

	local humanoid = self:GetLocalHumanoid()
	if humanoid and humanoid.Torso and #currentPoints >= 1 then
		local dist = (currentPoints[1] - humanoid.Torso.Position).magnitude
		expectedTimeToNextPoint = dist / humanoid.WalkSpeed
	end

	movementUpdateEvent:Fire("targetPoint", self.currentDestination)
end

function VRNavigation:GoToPoint(point)
	currentPath = true
	currentPoints = { point }
	currentPointIdx = 1
	moving = true

	local humanoid = self:GetLocalHumanoid()
	local distance = (humanoid.Torso.Position - point).magnitude
	local estimatedTimeRemaining = distance / humanoid.WalkSpeed

	timeReachedLastPoint = tick()
	expectedTimeToNextPoint = estimatedTimeRemaining

	movementUpdateEvent:Fire("targetPoint", point)
end

function VRNavigation:StopFollowingPath()
	currentPath = nil
	currentPoints = nil
	currentPointIdx = 0
	moving = false
	self.moveVector = ZERO_VECTOR3
end

function VRNavigation:TryComputePath(startPos, destination)
	local numAttempts = 0
	local newPath = nil

	while not newPath and numAttempts < 5 do
		newPath = PathfindingService:ComputeSmoothPathAsync(startPos, destination, MAX_PATHING_DISTANCE)
		numAttempts = numAttempts + 1

		if newPath.Status == Enum.PathStatus.ClosestNoPath or newPath.Status == Enum.PathStatus.ClosestOutOfRange then
			newPath = nil
			break
		end

		if newPath and newPath.Status == Enum.PathStatus.FailStartNotEmpty then
			startPos = startPos + (destination - startPos).unit
			newPath = nil
		end

		if newPath and newPath.Status == Enum.PathStatus.FailFinishNotEmpty then
			destination = destination + Vector3.new(0, 1, 0)
			newPath = nil
		end
	end

	return newPath
end

function VRNavigation:OnNavigationRequest(destinationCFrame, inputUserCFrame )
	local destinationPosition = destinationCFrame.p
	local lastDestination = self.currentDestination

	if not IsFiniteVector3(destinationPosition) then
		return
	end

	self.currentDestination = destinationPosition

	local humanoid = self:GetLocalHumanoid()
	if not humanoid or not humanoid.Torso then
		return
	end

	local currentPosition = humanoid.Torso.Position
	local distanceToDestination = (self.currentDestination - currentPosition).magnitude

	if distanceToDestination < NO_PATH_THRESHOLD then
		self:GoToPoint(self.currentDestination)
		return
	end

	if not lastDestination or (self.currentDestination - lastDestination).magnitude > RECALCULATE_PATH_THRESHOLD then
		local newPath = self:TryComputePath(currentPosition, self.currentDestination)
		if newPath then
			self:StartFollowingPath(newPath)
			if PathDisplay then
				PathDisplay.setCurrentPoints(self.currentPoints)
				PathDisplay.renderPath()
			end
		else
			self:StopFollowingPath()
			if PathDisplay then
				PathDisplay.clearRenderedPath()
			end
		end
	else
		if moving then
			self.currentPoints[#currentPoints] = self.currentDestination
		else
			self:GoToPoint(self.currentDestination)
		end
	end
end

function VRNavigation:OnJumpAction(actionName, inputState, inputObj)
	if inputState == Enum.UserInputState.Begin then
		self.isJumping = true
	end
	return Enum.ContextActionResult.Sink
end
function VRNavigation:BindJumpAction(active)
	if active then
		if not self.isJumpBound then
			self.isJumpBound = true
			ContextActionService:BindActionAtPriority("VRJumpAction", (function() return self:OnJumpAction() end), false,
				self.CONTROL_ACTION_PRIORITY, Enum.KeyCode.ButtonA)
		end
	else
		if self.isJumpBound then
			self.isJumpBound = false
			ContextActionService:UnbindAction("VRJumpAction")
		end
	end
end

function VRNavigation:ControlCharacterGamepad(actionName, inputState, inputObject)
	if inputObject.KeyCode ~= Enum.KeyCode.Thumbstick1 then return end

	if inputState == Enum.UserInputState.Cancel then
		self.moveVector =  ZERO_VECTOR3
		return
	end

	if inputState ~= Enum.UserInputState.End then
		self:StopFollowingPath()
		if PathDisplay then
			PathDisplay.clearRenderedPath()
		end

		if self:ShouldUseNavigationLaser() then
			self:BindJumpAction(true)
			self:SetLaserPointerMode("Hidden")
		end

		if inputObject.Position.magnitude > THUMBSTICK_DEADZONE then
			self.moveVector = Vector3.new(inputObject.Position.X, 0, -inputObject.Position.Y)
			if self.moveVector.magnitude > 0 then
				self.moveVector = self.moveVector.unit * math.min(1, inputObject.Position.magnitude)
			end

			self.moveLatch = true
		end
	else
		self.moveVector =  ZERO_VECTOR3

		if self:ShouldUseNavigationLaser() then
			self:BindJumpAction(false)
			self:SetLaserPointerMode("Navigation")
		end

		if self.moveLatch then
			self.moveLatch = false
			movementUpdateEvent:Fire("offtrack")
		end
	end
	return Enum.ContextActionResult.Sink
end

function VRNavigation:OnHeartbeat(dt)
	local newMoveVector = self.moveVector
	local humanoid = self:GetLocalHumanoid()
	if not humanoid or not humanoid.Torso then
		return
	end

	if self.moving and self.currentPoints then
		local currentPosition = humanoid.Torso.Position
		local goalPosition = currentPoints[1]
		local vectorToGoal = (goalPosition - currentPosition) * XZ_VECTOR3
		local moveDist = vectorToGoal.magnitude
		local moveDir = vectorToGoal / moveDist

		if moveDist < POINT_REACHED_THRESHOLD then
			local estimatedTimeRemaining = 0
			local prevPoint = currentPoints[1]
			for i, point in pairs(currentPoints) do
				if i ~= 1 then
					local dist = (point - prevPoint).magnitude
					prevPoint = point
					estimatedTimeRemaining = estimatedTimeRemaining + (dist / humanoid.WalkSpeed)
				end
			end

			table.remove(currentPoints, 1)
			currentPointIdx = currentPointIdx + 1

			if #currentPoints == 0 then
				self:StopFollowingPath()
				if PathDisplay then
					PathDisplay.clearRenderedPath()
				end
				return
			else
				if PathDisplay then
					PathDisplay.setCurrentPoints(currentPoints)
					PathDisplay.renderPath()
				end

				local newGoal = currentPoints[1]
				local distanceToGoal = (newGoal - currentPosition).magnitude
				expectedTimeToNextPoint = distanceToGoal / humanoid.WalkSpeed
				timeReachedLastPoint = tick()
			end
		else
			local ignoreTable = {
				game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character,
				workspace.CurrentCamera
			}
			local obstructRay = Ray.new(currentPosition - Vector3.new(0, 1, 0), moveDir * 3)
			local obstructPart, obstructPoint, obstructNormal = workspace:FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList(obstructRay, ignoreTable)

			if obstructPart then
				local heightOffset = Vector3.new(0, 100, 0)
				local jumpCheckRay = Ray.new(obstructPoint + moveDir * 0.5 + heightOffset, -heightOffset)
				local jumpCheckPart, jumpCheckPoint, jumpCheckNormal = workspace:FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList(jumpCheckRay, ignoreTable)

				local heightDifference = jumpCheckPoint.Y - currentPosition.Y
				if heightDifference < 6 and heightDifference > -2 then
					humanoid.Jump = true
				end
			end

			local timeSinceLastPoint = tick() - timeReachedLastPoint
			if timeSinceLastPoint > expectedTimeToNextPoint + OFFTRACK_TIME_THRESHOLD then
				self:StopFollowingPath()
				if PathDisplay then
					PathDisplay.clearRenderedPath()
				end

				movementUpdateEvent:Fire("offtrack")
			end

			newMoveVector = self.moveVector:Lerp(moveDir, dt * 10)
		end
	end

	if IsFiniteVector3(newMoveVector) then
		self.moveVector = newMoveVector
	end
end


function VRNavigation:OnUserCFrameEnabled()
	if self:ShouldUseNavigationLaser() then
		self:BindJumpAction(false)
		self:SetLaserPointerMode("Navigation")
	else
		self:BindJumpAction(true)
		self:SetLaserPointerMode("Hidden")
	end
end

function VRNavigation:Enable(enable)

	self.moveVector = ZERO_VECTOR3
	self.isJumping = false

	if enable then
		self.navigationRequestedConn = VRService.NavigationRequested:Connect(function(destinationCFrame, inputUserCFrame) self:OnNavigationRequest(destinationCFrame, inputUserCFrame) end)
		self.heartbeatConn = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt) self:OnHeartbeat(dt) end)

		ContextActionService:BindAction("MoveThumbstick", (function(actionName, inputState, inputObject) return self:ControlCharacterGamepad(actionName, inputState, inputObject) end),
			false, self.CONTROL_ACTION_PRIORITY, Enum.KeyCode.Thumbstick1)
		ContextActionService:BindActivate(Enum.UserInputType.Gamepad1, Enum.KeyCode.ButtonR2)

		self.userCFrameEnabledConn = VRService.UserCFrameEnabled:Connect(function() self:OnUserCFrameEnabled() end)
		self:OnUserCFrameEnabled()

		VRService:SetTouchpadMode(Enum.VRTouchpad.Left, Enum.VRTouchpadMode.VirtualThumbstick)
		VRService:SetTouchpadMode(Enum.VRTouchpad.Right, Enum.VRTouchpadMode.ABXY)

		self.enabled = true
	else
		-- Disable
		self:StopFollowingPath()

		ContextActionService:UnbindAction("MoveThumbstick")
		ContextActionService:UnbindActivate(Enum.UserInputType.Gamepad1, Enum.KeyCode.ButtonR2)

		self:BindJumpAction(false)
		self:SetLaserPointerMode("Disabled")

		if self.navigationRequestedConn then
			self.navigationRequestedConn:Disconnect()
			self.navigationRequestedConn = nil
		end
		if self.heartbeatConn then
			self.heartbeatConn:Disconnect()
			self.heartbeatConn = nil
		end
		if self.userCFrameEnabledConn then
			self.userCFrameEnabledConn:Disconnect()
			self.userCFrameEnabledConn = nil
		end
		self.enabled = false
	end
end

return VRNavigation

local Notification;

local RAY_DIRECTION = Vector3.new(0, -100, 0);

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local rootPart;
local MapGUI;
local lastDetectedArea;

local raycastParams = RaycastParams.new()
raycastParams.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Whitelist;
raycastParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = {workspace:WaitForChild('Areas')};

local RaycastWithWhitelist;

local AreaController = {Location = nil}

function AreaController:CharacterAdded(char)
    if not char then return; end;
    rootPart = char:WaitForChild('HumanoidRootPart');
end;

function AreaController:Start()

	local UI = localPlayer.PlayerGui.BottomLeftGUI;
	local AreaText = UI.MainFrame.AreaText;

    repeat task.wait() until rootPart

    while true do
        debug.profilebegin('AreaCheck');
        local raycastResult = RaycastWithWhitelist(rootPart.Position, RAY_DIRECTION, raycastParams);
        if raycastResult then
            local area = raycastResult.Instance;
            if lastDetectedArea ~= area then
                lastDetectedArea = area;
				self.Location = area.Name;

				AreaText.Text = area.Name;

				-- if string.find(self.Location, 'Road') or string.find(self.Location, 'Lane') or string.find(self.Location, 'Street') or string.find(self.Location, 'Drive') then
                -- else
                --     Notification.new('New Area', area.Name);
				-- end
            end;
        end;
        debug.profileend();
        task.wait(0.5);
    end;
end;


function AreaController:Init()
    Notification = self.Controllers.UI.Notification;
	RaycastWithWhitelist = self.Shared.Raycast.CastWithWhitelist;
end;

return AreaController;

local NetworkController;

local boatObject;

local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera;

local BoatController = {}

function BoatController:Start()
    NetworkController.Connect('Boat', function(event, ...)
        if event == 'Enter' then
            boatObject = Boat.new(...);
            camera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Track;
        elseif event == 'Exit' then
            boatObject:DisconnectBoat();
            boatObject = nil;
        end;
    end);
end

function BoatController:Init()
    Boat = self:WrapModule(require(script:WaitForChild('Boat')));
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    FOVController = self.Controllers.FOVController;
    Trove = self.Shared.Trove;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Boat/BoatController_contents/Boat.lua ---

--[[
    Boat (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Boat → BoatController
    Parent: BoatController
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56

-- Boat
-- Khizzer
-- October 21, 2023

local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")

local Trove;
local KeybindController;
local BoatGUI;
local NetworkController;

local ConvertSpeed;
local Lerp;
local Map;

local beginInputState = Enum.UserInputState.Begin;

local MAX_STEER_FORCE = 1.5;
local MIN_STEER_FORCE = 0.3;

local Boat = {}
Boat.__index = Boat

function Boat.new(boat, isEmergencyBoat: boolean)
    local self = setmetatable({}, Boat)

    self.Trove = Trove.new();
    self.Boat = boat;
    self.Body = boat.Body;
    self.Hull = boat.Hull;
    self.Platform = self.Hull.Platform;
    self.Seat = self.Hull.VehicleSeat;
    self.Config = boat.Config;
    self.State = self.Config.State;

    self.Anchor = false;

    self.Speeds = require(self.Config.Modules.Speeds);
    self.MaxSpeed = self.Speeds.MaxSpeed;
    self.ReverseSpeed = self.Speeds.ReverseSpeed;

    self.IsEmergencyBoat = isEmergencyBoat;

    self.AngularVelocity = self.Platform.AngularVelocity :: AngularVelocity;
    self.LinearVelocity = self.Platform.LinearVelocity;

    BoatGUI:Enable(self);
    self:SetupListeners();

    return self;
end

function Boat:Throttle()
    debug.profilebegin('BoatThrottle');
    local seat = self.Seat :: VehicleSeat;
    local platform = self.Platform;

    local throttleFloat = seat.ThrottleFloat;

    local maxSpeed = self.MaxSpeed;
    local maxReverseSpeed = self.ReverseSpeed;

    local targetSpeed = 0;

    if not self.Boat:GetAttribute('Engine') then
        self.LinearVelocity.LineVelocity = Lerp(self.LinearVelocity.LineVelocity, 0, 0.05);
        return;
    end;

    if self.Anchor then return; end;

    -- TODO: Do not allow boats to be driven when not on water

    local currentVelocity = self.LinearVelocity.LineVelocity;
    local lerpSpeed = Lerp(currentVelocity, if throttleFloat == 1 then self.MaxSpeed else self.ReverseSpeed, if throttleFloat ~= 0 then 0.01 else 0);
    targetSpeed = math.clamp(lerpSpeed, self.ReverseSpeed, self.MaxSpeed);

    self.LinearVelocity.LineVelocity = targetSpeed;

    BoatGUI:SetThrottle(targetSpeed, maxSpeed, maxReverseSpeed);
    BoatGUI:SetSpeed(ConvertSpeed(platform.Velocity.Magnitude, true, true), ConvertSpeed(maxSpeed, true, true), ConvertSpeed(maxReverseSpeed, true, true));

    debug.profileend();
end;

function Boat:Steer()
    debug.profilebegin('BoatSteer');
    if self.Anchor then return; end;

    local angularVelocity: AngularVelocity = self.AngularVelocity;

    local seat = self.Seat :: VehicleSeat;
    local platform = self.Platform;

    if not self.Boat:GetAttribute('Engine') then
        angularVelocity.AngularVelocity = angularVelocity.AngularVelocity:Lerp(Vector3.zero, 0.05);
        return;
    end

    local steerForce = Map(platform.Velocity.Magnitude, 0, self.MaxSpeed, MIN_STEER_FORCE, MAX_STEER_FORCE);

    self.AngularVelocity.AngularVelocity = Vector3.new(0, steerForce * seat.SteerFloat, 0);
    debug.profileend();
end

function Boat.SetEngine(inputState)
	if inputState and inputState ~= beginInputState then return; end;
	NetworkController.Send('Boat', 'Engine');
end;

function Boat:SetAnchor(inputState)
    if inputState and inputState ~= beginInputState then return; end;
    if ConvertSpeed(self.Platform.Velocity.Magnitude, true, true) > 50 then return _G.AeroError('Your boat is moving too fast!'); end;

    if not self.Anchor then
        self.Anchor = true;

        self.LinearVelocity.LineVelocity = 0;
        self.AngularVelocity.AngularVelocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0);
        BoatGUI:SetAnchor(true);
        BoatGUI:SetThrottle(0, ConvertSpeed(self.MaxSpeed, true, true), ConvertSpeed(self.ReverseSpeed, true, true));
        BoatGUI:SetSpeed(0, ConvertSpeed(self.MaxSpeed, true, true), ConvertSpeed(self.ReverseSpeed, true, true));
        NetworkController.Send('Boat', 'Anchor' , true);

    else
        self.Anchor = false;
        BoatGUI:SetAnchor(false);
        NetworkController.Send('Boat', 'Anchor' , false);
    end
end

function Boat:SetupListeners()
    local trove = self.Trove;

    local body = self.Body;

    local config = self.Config;

    do
        local gasConfig = config.Gas;
        local gas: Configuration = gasConfig:GetAttribute('Gas');
        local maxGas = gasConfig:GetAttribute('MaxGas') or 100;

        BoatGUI:SetGas(gas, maxGas);

        trove:Add(gasConfig:GetAttributeChangedSignal('Gas'):Connect(function()
            local _gas = gasConfig:GetAttribute('Gas');
            BoatGUI:SetGas(_gas, maxGas);
        end));
    end

    trove:Add(RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
        self:Throttle();
        self:Steer();
    end))

    trove:Add(self.Boat:GetAttributeChangedSignal('Engine'):Connect(function()
        local engineStatus: boolean = self.Boat:GetAttribute('Engine');

        BoatGUI:SetIgnition(engineStatus);

        if engineStatus then
            BoatGUI:SetThrottle(0, ConvertSpeed(self.MaxSpeed, true, true), ConvertSpeed(self.ReverseSpeed, true, true));
        end
        if config.Modules:FindFirstChild('Propellers') then
            local module = require(config.Modules.Propellers);
            module(body, engineStatus);
        end;
    end));

    do
        local navigationLightsState = self.State:GetAttribute('NavigationLights');
        BoatGUI:SetNavigationLights(navigationLightsState);
        trove:Add(self.State:GetAttributeChangedSignal('NavigationLights'):Connect(function()
            local _navigationLightsState = self.State:GetAttribute('NavigationLights');
            BoatGUI:SetNavigationLights(_navigationLightsState);
        end));
    end

    ----------------------
	trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
		ActionName = 'Engine';
		Key = Enum.KeyCode.K;
		Description = 'Engine';
		OnPressed = function(...)
			self.SetEngine(...);
		end;
	}));

    trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
		ActionName = 'Anchor';
		Key = Enum.KeyCode.G;
		AdditionalKeys = { Enum.KeyCode.P };
		Description = 'Anchor';
		OnPressed = function(...)
			self:SetAnchor(...);
		end;
	}));

    trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
        ActionName = 'NavigationLights';
        Key = Enum.KeyCode.L;
        Description = 'Navigation Lights';
        OnPressed = function()
            NetworkController.Send('Boat', 'NavigationLights');
        end;
    }))

    if self.IsEmergencyBoat then
        trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
            ActionName = 'ELS';
            Key = Enum.KeyCode.J;
            Description = 'Emergency Lights';
            OnPressed = function()
                NetworkController.Send('Boat', 'ELS');
            end;
        }))

        local sounds = self.Platform.Sounds;
        if sounds:FindFirstChild('Siren') then
            trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
                ActionName = 'Siren';
                Key = Enum.KeyCode.N;
                Description = 'Siren';
                OnPressed = function()
                    NetworkController.Send('Boat', 'Siren');
                end;
            }));
        end;
    end;
end


function Boat:DisconnectBoat()
    self.Trove:Destroy();
    BoatGUI:Disable();
end

function Boat:Init()
    Trove = self.Shared.Trove;
    Map = self.Shared.Map;
    KeybindController = self.Controllers.KeybindController;
    Lerp = self.Shared.MathUtil.Lerp;
    BoatGUI = self.Controllers.Boat.BoatGUI;
    ConvertSpeed = self.Shared.ConvertSpeed;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end


return Boat

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Boat/BoatGUI.lua ---

--[[
    BoatGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Boat
    Parent: Boat
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local StarterPack = game:GetService("StarterPack")
local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")

local BoatGUI = {}

local Trove
local Map;

local MIN_ROTATION = -143;
local MAX_ROTATION = 81;
local ENABLED_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
local DISABLED_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local WHITE_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255);

local TransmissionStates = {
  Drive = 1,
  Neutral = 0,
  Reverse = -1,
}

local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(0.23, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out);

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local gui: ScreenGui & { MainFrame: Frame } = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild("BoatGUI")
local main = gui.MainFrame
local buttonsFrame = main.ButtonsFrame;

local speedometer = main.SpeedometerMainFrame.SpeedometerFrame
local speedNeedle: Frame = speedometer.NeedleFrame
local speedLabel: TextLabel = speedometer.SpeedLabel

local gasFrame = main.GasMainFrame.GasFrame
local gasNeedle: Frame = gasFrame.NeedleFrame

local anchorBtn: ImageButton = buttonsFrame.AnchorBtn
local lightBtn: ImageButton = buttonsFrame.LightBtn
local ignitionBtn: ImageButton = buttonsFrame.IgnitionBtn
local lockBtn: ImageButton = buttonsFrame.LockBtn

local throttleSlider = main.ThrottleSlider
local throttleBar: Frame = throttleSlider.Frame

local rightControls: Frame & {
  ELSFrame: ImageLabel,
  SpotlightFrame: ImageLabel,
} = main.RightControlsFrame
local elsFrame = rightControls.ELSFrame
local spotlightFrame = rightControls.SpotlightFrame

local dialTweensCompleted = false
local lastGasAmount = 0
local lastMaxGas = 0
local trove
local activeBoat

-- TODO: Are boats having sirens? I don't think so??
local function AddSiren(name)
  -- Connects a siren
end

local function SetELSBtn(id, tbl) end

function BoatGUI:SetSpeed(val: number, max: number)
  if not dialTweensCompleted then return end
  val, max = math.abs(val), math.abs(max)
  speedNeedle.Rotation = Map(val, 0, max, MIN_ROTATION, MAX_ROTATION)
  speedLabel.Text = `{math.floor(val)} Knots` -- TODO: double check this is in the right unit
end

function BoatGUI:SetThrottle(val: number, max: number, maxReverse: number)
  --if not dialTweensCompleted then return end
  -- do we really need to do this

  if val > 0 then
    throttleBar.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, Map(val, 0, max, 0.75, 0), 0)
  elseif val < 0 then
    throttleBar.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, Map(val, 0, maxReverse, 0.75, 1), 0)
  else
    throttleBar.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.75, 0)
  end
end

function BoatGUI:SetGas(val: number, max: number, dontCache: boolean?)
  if dontCache ~= true then
    lastGasAmount = val
    lastMaxGas = max
  end
  if not dialTweensCompleted then return end
  gasNeedle.Rotation = Map(val, 0, max, MIN_ROTATION, MAX_ROTATION);
end

function BoatGUI:SetIgnition(enabled: boolean)
  if enabled then
    TweenService:Create(ignitionBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = ENABLED_COLOR}):Play()
    local startSpeedometerTween = TweenService:Create(speedNeedle, TweenInfo.new(1, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, 0, true), {Rotation = MAX_ROTATION})
    startSpeedometerTween.Completed:Once(function()
      dialTweensCompleted = true
    end)

    local startGasTween = TweenService:Create(gasNeedle, TweenInfo.new(1, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, 0, true), {Rotation = MAX_ROTATION})
    startGasTween.Completed:Once(function()
      dialTweensCompleted = true
      BoatGUI:SetGas(lastGasAmount, lastMaxGas)
    end)

    startSpeedometerTween:Play()
    startGasTween:Play()
  else
    TweenService:Create(ignitionBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = WHITE_COLOR}):Play()

    local stopSpeedTween = TweenService:Create(speedNeedle, TweenInfo.new(1, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, 0), {Rotation = MIN_ROTATION});
    stopSpeedTween:Play();
    stopSpeedTween.Completed:Once(function()
      dialTweensCompleted = false;
      stopSpeedTween:Destroy();
      stopSpeedTween = nil;
    end)
    
    
    local stopGasTween = TweenService:Create(gasNeedle, TweenInfo.new(1, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, 0), {Rotation = MIN_ROTATION});
    stopGasTween:Play();

    stopGasTween.Completed:Once(function()
      dialTweensCompleted = false;
      stopGasTween:Destroy();
      stopGasTween = nil;
    end)

    speedLabel.Text = '0 Knots';

    local throttleBarTween = TweenService:Create(throttleBar, TweenInfo.new(1, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, 0), {Position = UDim2.new(0.5, 0, 0.75, 0)});
    throttleBarTween:Play();
    throttleBarTween.Completed:Once(function()
      throttleBarTween:Destroy();
      throttleBarTween = nil;
    end);
  end
end

function BoatGUI:SetAnchor(enabled: boolean)
  TweenService:Create(anchorBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = enabled and ENABLED_COLOR or WHITE_COLOR}):Play()
end

function BoatGUI:SetNavigationLights(enabled: boolean)
  TweenService:Create(lightBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = enabled and ENABLED_COLOR or WHITE_COLOR}):Play()
end

function BoatGUI:SetLock(enabled: boolean)
  TweenService:Create(lockBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = enabled and ENABLED_COLOR or WHITE_COLOR}):Play()
end

function BoatGUI:Enable(boat)
  if activeBoat then
    BoatGUI:Disable()
  end

  if not trove then
    trove = Trove.new()
    trove:AttachToInstance(gui)
  end

  activeBoat = boat

  --elsFrame.Visible = activeBoat.IsEmergencyBoat
  spotlightFrame.Visible = false

  gui.Enabled = true
end

function BoatGUI:Disable()
  gui.Enabled = false

  if trove then
    trove:Clean()
  end

  -- BoatGUI:SetSpeed(0, 0)
  BoatGUI:SetGas(0, 0)
  -- [CarGui] SetELSBtn(0, patternBtns)
  -- [CarGui] Destroy siren buttons and clear selectedSirens

  activeBoat = nil
end

function BoatGUI:Init()
  Trove = self.Shared.Trove
  Map = self.Shared.Map
end

function BoatGUI:Start()
  -- BoatGUI:Enable()
end

return BoatGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Boat/BoatReplicationController.lua ---

--[[
    BoatReplicationController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Boat
    Parent: Boat
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
-- Boat Replication Controller
-- Khizzer
-- January 23, 2024

local NavigationLights;
local ELS;

local timeSinceLastUpdate = 1;

local MAX_REPLICATION_DISTANCE = 2000;
local UPDATE_COOLDOWN = 0.1;

local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera;

local GetSeatOccupant;
local Map;

local boatsFolder = workspace:WaitForChild('Boats');

local function SetupBoatEffects(boat: Model)
    local hull = boat:WaitForChild('Hull');

    local config = boat:WaitForChild('Config');

    do
        local function Check()
            local navigationLightsState: boolean = config.State:GetAttribute('NavigationLights');
            NavigationLights.Set(boat, navigationLightsState);
        end;
        pcall(Check);
        config.State:GetAttributeChangedSignal('NavigationLights'):Connect(Check);
    end;

    do
        local elsModelValue = config:FindFirstChild('ELS');
        local function Check()
            if elsModelValue then
                local elsPatternModule = config.Modules.ELSPattern;
                local elsState = config.State:GetAttribute('ELS');
                if elsState == true then
                    ELS.Enable(elsModelValue.Value, elsPatternModule);
                end
            end;
        end;
        pcall(Check);
        config.State:GetAttributeChangedSignal('ELS'):Connect(Check);
    end;
end

local BoatReplicationController = {}

function BoatReplicationController:Start()
    for _,v in next, boatsFolder:GetChildren() do
        task.defer(SetupBoatEffects, v);
    end;

    boatsFolder.ChildAdded:Connect(function(boat)
        task.defer(SetupBoatEffects, boat);
    end);

    RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
        timeSinceLastUpdate += dt;
        if timeSinceLastUpdate < UPDATE_COOLDOWN then return; end;
        timeSinceLastUpdate = 0;

        for _,v in next, workspace.Boats:GetChildren() do
            local hull: Model? = v:FindFirstChild('Hull');
            if not hull then return; end;

            local platform: Part? = hull:FindFirstChild('Platform');
            if not platform then return; end;

            if (camera.CFrame.Position - platform.Position).Magnitude  > MAX_REPLICATION_DISTANCE then continue; end;

            local seat = hull:FindFirstChildOfClass('VehicleSeat');
            if not seat then continue; end;

            local magnitude = platform.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Magnitude;
            local sounds = platform.Sounds;

            if seat:FindFirstChild('SeatWeld') then
                local playbackSpeed = math.min(0.5 + ((magnitude / 110) * 0.6), 1.1);
                sounds.Engine.PlaybackSpeed = playbackSpeed;

                local volume = math.min(0.3 + ((magnitude / 110) * 0.6), 0.8);
                sounds.Engine.Volume = volume;
            else
                sounds.Engine.PlaybackSpeed = 0.5;
                sounds.Engine.Volume = 0.3;
            end;
            --TODO: Background sound
        end

    end)

    --TODO: Handle boat deletion
end

function BoatReplicationController:Init()
    Map = self.Shared.MathUtil.Map;
    NavigationLights = self:WrapModule(require(script:WaitForChild('NavigationLights')));
    ELS = self:WrapModule(require(script:WaitForChild('ELS')));
end


return BoatReplicationController

--[[
    ELS (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Boat → BoatReplicationController
    Parent: BoatReplicationController
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- ELS
-- Khizzer
-- January 27, 2024


local ELS = {}

local coroutineWrap = coroutine.wrap;
local pcall = pcall;
local error = error;

function ELS.Enable(ELSModel, elsModule)
    local PatternFunc = require(elsModule);
    local enabled = true;

    if not ELSModel then warn(elsModule:GetFullName().. ' - This vehicle has no ELS object value!') end;

    local function ModifiedWait(duration)
        if not enabled then error(); end;
        task.wait(duration);
        if not enabled then error(); end;
    end;

    coroutineWrap(function()
        pcall(PatternFunc, ELSModel, enabled, ModifiedWait);
    end)();

    coroutineWrap(function()
        elsModule.Parent.Parent.State:GetAttributeChangedSignal('ELS'):Wait();

        enabled = false;
        pcall(PatternFunc, ELSModel, enabled, ModifiedWait);

        PatternFunc = nil;
        ModifiedWait = nil;
    end)();
end;


return ELS

-- Boat Spawner Controller
-- Khizzer
-- February 17, 2024

local BoatSpawnerModel;
local BoatSpawnerGUI;
local NetworkController;
local NetworkFunctionController;

local CAMERA_OFFSET = CFrame.new(10, 1.5, 0);
local BUY_BOAT_EVENT;
local SPAWN_BOAT_EVENT;

local BoatSpawnerController = {}

function BoatSpawnerController.SetupCameraAndGetViewportBoat(camera, boatID)
    local boat = BoatSpawnerModel:GetBoatFromID(boatID):Clone();

    camera.CFrame = CFrame.new((boat.PrimaryPart.CFrame * CAMERA_OFFSET).Position, boat.PrimaryPart.Position);

    return boat;
end;

function BoatSpawnerController.SpawnBoat(boatID)
    NetworkController.Send(SPAWN_BOAT_EVENT, boatID);
    BoatSpawnerGUI.Disable();
end;

function BoatSpawnerController.BuyBoat(boatID)
    return NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer(BUY_BOAT_EVENT, boatID);
end;

function BoatSpawnerController.HasBoughtBoat(boatID)
    return NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('HasBoughtBoat', boatID);
end;

function BoatSpawnerController.GetBoatPriceFromID(boatID)
    return BoatSpawnerModel:GetBoatPriceFromID(boatID);
end;

function BoatSpawnerController.GetBoatInfo()
    return BoatSpawnerModel:GetBoatInfo();
end;

function BoatSpawnerController.GetBoatInfoForCategory(category: string)
    return BoatSpawnerModel:GetBoatInfoForCategory(category);
end;

function BoatSpawnerController:Init()
    NetworkFunctionController = self.Controllers.NetworkFunctionController;
    BoatSpawnerModel = self.Controllers.BoatSpawner.BoatSpawnerModel;
    BoatSpawnerGUI = self.Controllers.BoatSpawner.BoatSpawnerGUI;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    local constants = self.Shared.Constants.BoatSpawner;
    BUY_BOAT_EVENT = constants.BUY_BOAT_EVENT;
	SPAWN_BOAT_EVENT = constants.SPAWN_BOAT_EVENT;
end;


return BoatSpawnerController

--[[
    BoatSpawnerGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → BoatSpawner
    Parent: BoatSpawner

]]
-- Boat SpawnerGUI
-- Khizzer
-- February 17, 2024

local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local BoatSpawnerController;
local Trove;

local GuiTrove;

local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);
local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
local PRICE_PREFIX = '$';

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local boatSpawnerGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('BoatSpawnerGUI');
local mainFrame = boatSpawnerGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;

local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local exitBtn = btnsFrame.ExitBtn;
local buyBtn = btnsFrame.BuyBtn;
local spawnBtn = btnsFrame.SpawnBtn;

local boatsListScrollingFrame = bodyFrame.BoatsListImage.BoatsListScrollingFrame;
local packageListScrollingFrame = bodyFrame.BoatsListImage.PackageListScrollingFrame;

local detailsFrame = bodyFrame.DetailsFrame;
local boatViewportFrame = detailsFrame.BoatViewportFrame;
local nameLabel = detailsFrame.NameLabel;
local priceLabel = detailsFrame.PriceLabel;

local components = boatSpawnerGUI.Components;
local boatBtnPrefab = components.BoatBtn;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

local selectedBtn;

local buyConnection;
local spawnConnection;

local viewportCamera;
local viewportBoatModel;

local function CreateCamera()
    local camera = Instance.new('Camera');
    return camera;
end;

local BoatSpawnerGUI = {}

function BoatSpawnerGUI.IsEnabled()
    return boatSpawnerGUI.Enabled;
end;

function BoatSpawnerGUI.Enable()
    if GuiTrove then GuiTrove:Destroy(); end;
    
    GuiTrove = Trove.new();


    viewportCamera = CreateCamera();
    boatViewportFrame.CurrentCamera = viewportCamera;
    boatsListScrollingFrame.Visible = true;
    packageListScrollingFrame.Visible = false;

    for i,v in next, BoatSpawnerController.GetBoatInfo() do
        if typeof(i) ~= "string" then
            local boatName = v.Name;
            local boatID = v.ID;

            local boatBtn = boatBtnPrefab:Clone();
            boatBtn.BoatLabel.Text = boatName;
            boatBtn.Parent = boatsListScrollingFrame;

            GuiTrove:Add(boatBtn);

            local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(boatBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {BackgroundColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
            local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(boatBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {BackgroundColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
            local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(boatBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {BackgroundColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

            GuiTrove:Add(hoverTween);
            GuiTrove:Add(hoverEndTween);
            GuiTrove:Add(selectedTween);

            local function ReloadBuyandSpawnBtn()
                local hasBoughtBoat = BoatSpawnerController.HasBoughtboat(boatID)
                buyBtn.Visible = not hasBoughtBoat;
                spawnBtn.Visible = hasBoughtBoat;
            end;

            GuiTrove:Add(boatBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                hoverTween:Play();
            end));

            GuiTrove:Add(boatBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                hoverEndTween:Play();
            end));

            GuiTrove:Add(boatBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                if selectedBtn then
                    TweenService:Create(selectedBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
                end;

                selectedBtn = boatBtn;
                selectedTween:Play();

                nameLabel.Text = boatName;
                priceLabel.Text = PRICE_PREFIX .. BoatSpawnerController.GetBoatPriceFromID(boatID);

                if viewportBoatModel then
                    viewportBoatModel:Destroy();
                end;

                viewportBoatModel = BoatSpawnerController.SetupCameraAndGetViewportBoat(viewportCamera, boatID);
                viewportBoatModel.Parent = boatViewportFrame;

                ReloadBuyandSpawnBtn();

                if buyConnection then
                    buyConnection:Disconnect();
                end;

                if spawnConnection then
                    spawnConnection:Disconnect();
                end;

                buyConnection = buyBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    BoatSpawnerController.BuyBoat(boatID);
                    ReloadBuyandSpawnBtn();
                end);

                spawnConnection = spawnBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    BoatSpawnerController.SpawnBoat(boatID);
                end);
            end))
        else
            if #BoatSpawnerController.GetCarInfoForCategory(i) == 0 then
                continue;
            end;

            local categoryBtn = boatBtnPrefab:Clone();
            categoryBtn.BoatLabel.Text = i;
            categoryBtn.Parent = packageListScrollingFrame;

            local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(categoryBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {BackgroundColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
            local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(categoryBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {BackgroundColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});

            GuiTrove:Add(categoryBtn);
            GuiTrove:Add(hoverTween);
            GuiTrove:Add(hoverEndTween);

            GuiTrove:Add(categoryBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                hoverTween:Play();
            end));

            GuiTrove:Add(categoryBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                hoverEndTween:Play();
            end));

            GuiTrove:Add(categoryBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                boatsListScrollingFrame.Visible = false;
                packageListScrollingFrame.Visible = true;

                if buyConnection then
                    buyConnection:Disconnect();
                end;

                if spawnConnection then
                    spawnConnection:Disconnect();
                end;

                local backBtn = boatBtnPrefab:Clone();
                backBtn.BoatLabel.Text = 'Back';
                backBtn.Parent = packageListScrollingFrame;

                GuiTrove:Add(backBtn);

                GuiTrove:Add(backBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    for _,v3 in packageListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
                        if v3:IsA('TextButton') then
                            v3:Destroy();
                        end;
                    end;

                    boatsListScrollingFrame.Visible = true;
                    packageListScrollingFrame.Visible = false;
                end));

                for i2, v2 in BoatSpawnerController.GetCarInfoForCategory(i) do
                    local boatName = v2.Name;
                    local boatID = v2.ID;

                    local boatBtn = boatBtnPrefab:Clone();
                    boatBtn.BoatLabel.Text = boatName;
                    boatBtn.Parent = packageListScrollingFrame;

                    GuiTrove:Add(boatBtn);

                    local _hoverTween = TweenService:Create(boatBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {BackgroundColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
                    local _hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(boatBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {BackgroundColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
                    local _selectedTween = TweenService:Create(boatBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {BackgroundColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});
                    
                    GuiTrove:Add(_hoverTween);
                    GuiTrove:Add(_hoverEndTween);
                    GuiTrove:Add(_selectedTween);

                    local function ReloadBuyandSpawnBtn()
                        local hasBoughtBoat = BoatSpawnerController.HasBoughtBoat(boatID)
                        buyBtn.Visible = not hasBoughtBoat;
                        spawnBtn.Visible = hasBoughtBoat;
                    end;


                    GuiTrove:Add(boatBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                        if selectedBtn == boatBtn then return; end;
                        _hoverTween:Play();
                    end));

                    GuiTrove:Add(boatBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                        if selectedBtn == boatBtn then return; end;
                        _hoverEndTween:Play();
                    end));

                    GuiTrove:Add(boatBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                        if selectedBtn then
                            TweenService:Create(selectedBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
                        end;

                        selectedBtn = boatBtn;
                        _selectedTween:Play();

                        nameLabel.Text = boatName;
                        priceLabel.Text = PRICE_PREFIX .. BoatSpawnerController.GetBoatPriceFromID(boatID);

                        if viewportBoatModel then
                            viewportBoatModel:Destroy();
                        end;

                        viewportBoatModel = BoatSpawnerController.SetupCameraAndGetViewportBoat(viewportCamera, boatID);
                        viewportBoatModel.Parent = boatViewportFrame;

                        ReloadBuyandSpawnBtn();

                        if buyConnection then
                            buyConnection:Disconnect();
                        end;

                        if spawnConnection then
                            spawnConnection:Disconnect();
                        end;

                        buyConnection = buyBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                            BoatSpawnerController.BuyBoat(boatID);
                            ReloadBuyandSpawnBtn();
                        end);

                        spawnConnection = spawnBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                            BoatSpawnerController.SpawnBoat(boatID);
                            for _,v3 in packageListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
                                if v3:IsA('TextButton') then
                                    v3:Destroy();
                                end;
                            end;
                        end);
                    end))
                end
            end));
        end
    end

    boatSpawnerGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play();
end;

function BoatSpawnerGUI.Disable()
    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Wait();
    boatSpawnerGUI.Enabled = false;

    GuiTrove:Destroy();
    GuiTrove = nil;

    selectedBtn = nil;
    nameLabel.Text = '';
    priceLabel.Text = '';
    spawnBtn.Visible = false;
    buyBtn.Visible = false;
    boatViewportFrame.CurrentCamera = nil;
    if viewportCamera then
        viewportCamera:Destroy();
    end;
    if viewportBoatModel then
        viewportBoatModel:Destroy();
    end;
    if buyConnection then
        buyConnection:Disconnect();
        buyConnection = nil;
    end;
    if spawnConnection then
        spawnConnection:Disconnect();
        spawnConnection = nil;
    end;

    for i, v in next, boatsListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
            v:Destroy();
        end;
    end;

    for i,v in next, packageListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
            v:Destroy();
        end;
    end;
end;

function BoatSpawnerGUI:Init()
    Trove = self.Shared.Trove;
    BoatSpawnerController = self.Controllers.BoatSpawner.BoatSpawnerController;
end


return BoatSpawnerGUI

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/BoatSpawner/BoatSpawnerModel.lua ---

--[[
    BoatSpawnerModel (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → BoatSpawner
    Parent: BoatSpawner
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Boat Spawner Model
-- Khizzer
-- February 17, 2024

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;

local boats = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Boats");

local DeveloperCheck;

local BoatSpawnerModel = {}

function BoatSpawnerModel.GetBoatsFolderForLocalPlayer()
    local jobName = localPlayer:GetAttribute('CurrentJob');
    local division = localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division');
    local folder = (jobName and boats:FindFirstChild(jobName)) or (division and boats:FindFirstChild(division)) or boats:FindFirstChild(localPlayer.Team.Name)
    if folder:GetAttribute("Redirect") then
        local newFolder = boats:FindFirstChild(folder:GetAttribute("Redirect"))
        if not newFolder then
            warn(`Invalid redirect folder \`${folder:GetAttribute("Redirect")}\` for {folder.Name}`)
            return folder
        end
        return newFolder
    end
    return folder
end;

function BoatSpawnerModel:GetBoatFromID(boatID)
    local boatsFolder = self.GetBoatsFolderForLocalPlayer();
    for i, v in next, boatsFolder:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('Model') then
            local spawnerSettings = v.Config.SpawnerSettings;
            if spawnerSettings.ID.Value == boatID then
                return v;
            end;
        else
            for i2, v2 in next, v:GetChildren() do
                local spawnerSettings = v2.Config.SpawnerSettings;
                if spawnerSettings.ID.Value == boatID then
                    return v2;
                end;
            end;
        end;
    end;
end;

function BoatSpawnerModel:GetBoatPriceFromID(boatID)
    return self:GetBoatFromID(boatID).Config.SpawnerSettings.Price.Value;
end;

function BoatSpawnerModel:GetBoatInfo()
    local info = {};

    local proxySortedKeys = {};

    local BoatsFolderForLocalPlayer = {};

    --This sorts out the cars in order of price
    do
        for _,v in next, self.GetBoatsFolderForLocalPlayer():GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('Model') then
                table.insert(proxySortedKeys, v);
            end;
        end;

        table.sort(proxySortedKeys, function(a, b)
            local aPrice = a.Config.SpawnerSettings.Price.Value;
            local bPrice = b.Config.SpawnerSettings.Price.Value;

            if aPrice == bPrice then
                return a.Name < b.Name;
            end;

            return a.Config.SpawnerSettings.Price.Value < b.Config.SpawnerSettings.Price.Value;
        end);
    end;

    --Add the cars with different package selections to the bottom of the list (they are all police so it doesnt matter about price)
    do
        --For each car in the sorted keys, add it to the CarsFolderForLocalPlayer table
        for _,v in next, proxySortedKeys do
            table.insert(BoatsFolderForLocalPlayer, v);
        end;

        for _,v in next, self.GetBoatsFolderForLocalPlayer():GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('Folder') then
                table.insert(BoatsFolderForLocalPlayer, v);
            end;
        end;
    end

    for i, v in next, BoatsFolderForLocalPlayer do
        if v:IsA('Model') then
            local spawnerSettings = v.Config.SpawnerSettings;
            local groupID = spawnerSettings:FindFirstChild('GroupID');
            local minRank = groupID and spawnerSettings:FindFirstChild('MinRank');
            local condition = spawnerSettings:FindFirstChild('Condition');
            local conditionFunc = if condition then require(condition) else function() return false end;
            if (not minRank) or DeveloperCheck(localPlayer) or (localPlayer:GetRankInGroup(groupID.Value) >= minRank.Value) or conditionFunc(localPlayer) then
                table.insert(info, {
                    Name = v.Name,
                    ID = spawnerSettings.ID.Value
                });
            end;
        elseif v:IsA('Folder') then
            info[v.Name] = {};
            local carTable = info[v.Name];
            for _,car in next, v:GetChildren() do
                local spawnerSettings = car.Config.SpawnerSettings;
                local groupID = spawnerSettings:FindFirstChild('GroupID');
                local minRank = groupID and spawnerSettings:FindFirstChild('MinRank');
                local condition = spawnerSettings:FindFirstChild('Condition');
                local conditionFunc = if condition then require(condition) else function() return false end;
				if (not minRank) or DeveloperCheck(localPlayer) or (localPlayer:GetRankInGroup(groupID.Value) >= minRank.Value) or conditionFunc(localPlayer) then
                    table.insert(carTable, {
                        Name = car.Name,
                        ID = spawnerSettings.ID.Value
                    });
                end;
            end;
        end;
    end;
    return info;
end;

function BoatSpawnerModel:GetCarInfoForCategory(category: string)
    local info = {};
    for i, v in next, self.GetBoatsFolderForLocalPlayer()[category]:GetChildren() do
        local spawnerSettings = v.Config.SpawnerSettings;
        local groupID = spawnerSettings:FindFirstChild('GroupID');
        local minRank = groupID and spawnerSettings:FindFirstChild('MinRank');
		if (not minRank) or DeveloperCheck(localPlayer) or (localPlayer:GetRankInGroup(groupID.Value) >= minRank.Value) then
            table.insert(info, {
                Name = v.Name,
                ID = spawnerSettings.ID.Value
            });
        end
    end;
    return info;
end

function BoatSpawnerModel:Init()
    DeveloperCheck = self.Shared.DeveloperCheck;
end


return BoatSpawnerModel

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/BuildingLoader.lua ---

--[[
    BuildingLoader (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers
    Parent: Controllers
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:55
]]
-- BuildingLoader Controller
-- LG
-- June 21, 2021

local BuildingLoader = {};

local Players = game:GetService('Players');


local Areas = workspace:FindFirstChild('AreaLoader');
local DownDirection = Vector3.new(0, -70, 0);
local UnloadedAreaStorage = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage').AreaLoaderBuildings;
local LoadedAreaStorage = Areas.LoadedArea;
local CastWithWhitelist;

local CurrentArea

local localPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer;
local char;
local rootPart;

function BuildingLoader:CharacterAdded(_char)
	if not _char then return; end;
	char = _char;
	rootPart = char:WaitForChild('HumanoidRootPart');
end;


function BuildingLoader:Start()
	repeat task.wait() until rootPart;

	for _,v in LoadedAreaStorage:GetChildren() do
		v.Parent = UnloadedAreaStorage;
	end;

	while true do
		local Rootpart = rootPart;
		local IsHit = false
		local raycastParams = RaycastParams.new();
		raycastParams.FilterDescendantsInstances = {Areas.DetectionParts};
		raycastParams.FilterType = Enum.RaycastFilterType.Whitelist;

		local ray = workspace:Raycast(Rootpart.Position, DownDirection, raycastParams)
		local Hit;

		if ray then
			if ray.Instance then
				if ray.Instance:IsA('BasePart') then
					IsHit = true;
					Hit = ray.Instance;
				else
					IsHit = false;
				end;
			else
				IsHit = false;
			end;
		end;

		--print('[Area Loader] ', 'IsHit', IsHit, 'HitName', Hit and Hit.Name or 'nil');

		if IsHit and string.find(Hit.Name, 'Detection') then
			local AreaName = string.sub(Hit.Name, 1, -10)
			if not LoadedAreaStorage:FindFirstChild(AreaName) then
				CurrentArea = UnloadedAreaStorage:FindFirstChild(AreaName);
				if CurrentArea then
					CurrentArea.Parent = LoadedAreaStorage;
				end;
			end;
		elseif (not IsHit) or (IsHit and not string.find(Hit.Name, 'Detection')) then
			--Areas[Hit.Name].Parent = AreaInteriors;
			if CurrentArea then
				CurrentArea.Parent = UnloadedAreaStorage;
			end;
		end;
		task.wait(0.2);
	end;

end

function BuildingLoader:Init()
	--BuildingModule = self:WrapModule(require(script:WaitForChild('BuildingModule')))
	local Raycast = self.Shared.Raycast;
	CastWithWhitelist = Raycast.CastWithWhitelist;
end;


return BuildingLoader

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/BusinessClothingController.lua ---

--[[
    BusinessClothingController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers
    Parent: Controllers
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:55
]]
-- Business Clothing Controller
-- Khizzer
-- April 6, 2023



local BusinessClothingController = {}

local char;

local oldShirt;
local oldPants;

function BusinessClothingController:SetShirt(id)
    local shirt = char:FindFirstChildOfClass('Shirt');
    if shirt and not oldShirt then
        oldShirt = shirt.ShirtTemplate;
        shirt.ShirtTemplate = id;
    elseif shirt and oldShirt then
        shirt.ShirtTemplate = id;
    else
        shirt = Instance.new('Shirt');
        shirt.Parent = char;
        shirt.ShirtTemplate = id;
        shirt:SetAttribute('Destroy', true);
    end;
    char:SetAttribute('CanReset', true);
end

function BusinessClothingController:SetPants(id)
    local pants = char:FindFirstChildOfClass('Pants');
    if pants and not oldPants then
        oldPants = pants.PantsTemplate;
        pants.PantsTemplate = id;
    elseif pants and oldPants then
        pants.PantsTemplate = id;
    else
        pants = Instance.new('Pants');
        pants.Parent = char;
        pants.PantsTemplate = id;
        pants:SetAttribute('Destroy', true);
    end;
    char:SetAttribute('CanReset', true);
end;

function BusinessClothingController:ResetClothing()
    if not char:GetAttribute('CanReset') then return end;

    local shirt = char:FindFirstChildOfClass('Shirt');
    local pants = char:FindFirstChildOfClass('Pants');

    if oldShirt then
        shirt.ShirtTemplate = oldShirt;
    elseif shirt then
        if shirt:GetAttribute('Destroy') then
            shirt:Destroy();
        end;
    end;

    if oldPants then
        char:FindFirstChildOfClass('Pants').PantsTemplate = oldPants;
    elseif pants then
        if pants:GetAttribute('Destroy') then
            pants:Destroy();
        end;
    end;

    char:SetAttribute('CanReset', nil);
end

function BusinessClothingController:CharacterAdded(_char)
    char = _char;
    oldShirt = nil;
    oldPants = nil;
end;


function BusinessClothingController:Start()
	
end


function BusinessClothingController:Init()
	
end


return BusinessClothingController

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/CallsignController.lua ---

--[[
    CallsignController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers
    Parent: Controllers
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local NetworkController;
local CallsignGUI;
local TeamController;
local teamName;

local prefixes;

local CallsignController = {};

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local DivisionStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Divisions;

local GetEmergencyTeams;
local NetworkFunctionController;

function CallsignController.SetCallsign(callsign)
    local callsignWithPrefix;
    if localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division') ~= nil then
        local divisionName = localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division');
        callsignWithPrefix = prefixes[divisionName] .. callsign;
    else
        callsignWithPrefix = prefixes[teamName] .. callsign;
    end
    if NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('IsCallsignTaken', callsignWithPrefix) == true then
        return true;
    end;
    NetworkController.Send('SetCallsign', callsignWithPrefix);
    CallsignGUI:Disable();
end;

function CallsignController.HasRegisteredCallsign(teamName)
    return NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('HasRegisteredCallsign', teamName);
end;

function CallsignController:Start()
    TeamController.ListenForTeamChange(GetEmergencyTeams(), function(isOnTeam, _teamName)
        teamName = _teamName;
        if isOnTeam then
            CallsignGUI:Enable(teamName);
        else
            CallsignGUI:Disable(true);
        end;
    end);

    localPlayer:GetAttributeChangedSignal('Division'):Connect(function()
        local divisionName = localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division');
        if divisionName and DivisionStorage[localPlayer.Team.Name] then
            CallsignGUI:Enable(divisionName);
        else
            if GetEmergencyTeams()[localPlayer.Team.Name] and divisionName == nil then
                CallsignGUI:Enable(localPlayer.Team.Name);
            else
                CallsignGUI:Disable(true);
            end;
        end
    end)
end;

function CallsignController:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    NetworkFunctionController = self.Controllers.NetworkFunctionController
    CallsignGUI = self.Controllers.UI.CallsignGUI;
    TeamController = self.Controllers.TeamController;
    prefixes = self.Shared.CallsignPrefixes;
    GetEmergencyTeams = self.Shared.Constants.WhitelistedTeams.GetEmergencyTeams;
end;

return CallsignController;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Car/CarController.lua ---

--[[
    CarController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Car
    Parent: Car
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local ContextActionService = game:GetService('ContextActionService');

local Car;
local NetworkController;
local Raycast;
local FOVController;
local Maid;
local CarGUI;

local DEFAULT_FOV = 70;
local SHAKE_SPEED = 20;
local SHAKE_POWER = 0.0007;
local SPACE_KEYCODE = Enum.KeyCode.Space;
local BEGIN_INPUT_STATE = Enum.UserInputState.Begin;

local mathMin = math.min;
local mathCos = math.cos;
local mathSin = math.sin;
local tableFind = table.find;
local tableRemove = table.remove;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera;

local carModel;
local carObject;

local maid;

local postSimulation = game:GetService('RunService').Heartbeat;

local ignoreList = {};

local function GetCarFromDescendant(descendant)
    local currentInstance = descendant;
    repeat
        currentInstance = currentInstance.Parent;
        wait();
    until currentInstance:FindFirstChild('Chassis');
    return currentInstance;
end;

local function ShakeCamera()
    local t = tick();

    camera.CFrame = camera.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(
        mathCos(t * SHAKE_SPEED) * SHAKE_POWER,
        mathSin(t * SHAKE_SPEED) * SHAKE_POWER,
        0
    );
end;

local CarController = {};

function CarController:CharacterAdded(char)
    if not char then return; end;

    local humanoid = char:WaitForChild('Humanoid');

    humanoid:GetPropertyChangedSignal('SeatPart'):Connect(function()
        local seat = humanoid.SeatPart;
        if seat and seat:FindFirstAncestor('Cars') then
            do
                carModel = GetCarFromDescendant(seat);
                ignoreList[#ignoreList + 1] = carModel;
            end;

            do
                ContextActionService:BindAction('ExitCarSeat', function(actionName, inputState)
                    if inputState ~= BEGIN_INPUT_STATE then return; end;
                    local seatPos = seat.Position;
                    local hit = Raycast.FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList(seatPos, seat.Exit.WorldPosition - seatPos, {unpack(ignoreList), char});
                    if not localPlayer:GetAttribute('PlacedInVehicle') then
                        seat.SeatWeld:Destroy();
                    end
                    NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Exit', hit and true);
                end, true, SPACE_KEYCODE);

                ContextActionService:SetTitle('ExitCarSeat', 'Exit');
            end;

            do
                local charAncestryChanged;
                local seatAncestryChanged;
                maid:GiveTask(postSimulation:Connect(function()
                    local magnitude = seat.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Magnitude;

                    if magnitude > 78 then
                        debug.profilebegin('CarShakeCamera');
                        ShakeCamera();
                        debug.profileend();
                    end;

                    debug.profilebegin('CarFOV')
                    FOVController.SetFOV(mathMin(DEFAULT_FOV + (magnitude * 0.06), 100));
                    debug.profileend();
                end));
                local function AncestryChanged(child, parent)
                    if not parent then
                        maid:DoCleaning();

                        charAncestryChanged:Disconnect();
                        charAncestryChanged = nil;

                        seatAncestryChanged:Disconnect();
                        seatAncestryChanged = nil;
                    end;
                end;
                charAncestryChanged = char.AncestryChanged:Connect(AncestryChanged);
                seatAncestryChanged = seat.AncestryChanged:Connect(AncestryChanged);
            end;
        else
            do
                if carModel then
                    local tableIndex = tableFind(ignoreList, carModel);
                    if tableIndex then
                        tableRemove(ignoreList, tableIndex);
                    end;
                end;
            end;

            do
                ContextActionService:UnbindAction('ExitCarSeat');
            end;

            do
                maid:DoCleaning();
                FOVController.SetFOV(DEFAULT_FOV);
                camera.CameraSubject = humanoid;
            end;
        end;
    end);
end;

function CarController.ChangeGear(...)
    carObject:ChangeGear(...);
end;

function CarController.SetParkingBrake()
    carObject:SetParkingBrake();
end;

function CarController.Flip()
    carObject:Flip();
end;

function CarController.SetHeadlights()
    Car.SetHeadlights();
end;

function CarController.SetIndicator(...)
    Car.SetIndicator(...);
end;

function CarController.SetHazards()
    Car.SetHazards();
end;

function CarController.Honk()
    Car.Honk();
end;

function CarController.Lock()
    Car.Lock();
end;

function CarController.SetELSPattern(...)
    Car.SetELSPattern(...);
end;

function CarController.SetTDPattern(...)
    Car.SetTDPattern(...);
end

function CarController.SetSiren(...)
    Car.SetSiren(...);
end;

function CarController.LeaveCar()
    Car:DisconnectCar();
end;

function CarController.SpotlightMove(...)
    Car.MoveSpotlight(...);
end;

function CarController.SetEngine()
    Car.SetEngine(Enum.UserInputState.Begin);
end

function CarController.GetCar()
    return carObject;
end

function CarController.SpotlightToggle()
    Car:ToggleSpotlight();
    local car = localPlayer.Car.Value;
    if not car then return; end;
    local spotlightFolder = car.Config.State:FindFirstChild('Spotlight');
    if spotlightFolder then
        task.wait(0.15)
    	local toggleStatus = spotlightFolder.Toggle.Value;
    	CarGUI.UpdateSpotlightToggle(toggleStatus);
	end
end;

function CarController:Start()
    maid = Maid.new();

    NetworkController.Connect('Car', function(event, ...)
        if event == 'Enter' then
			carObject = Car.new(...);
			camera.CameraType = Enum.CameraType.Track;
        elseif event == 'Exit' then
			carObject:DisconnectCar();
        end;
    end);

    NetworkController.Connect('RADIO_MUFFLE', function(car, status)
        local muffleEffect = car.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Radio.Muffle;
        muffleEffect.Enabled = status;
    end)
end;

function CarController:Init()
    Car = self:WrapModule(require(script:WaitForChild('Car')));
    CarGUI = self.Controllers.Car.CarGUI;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    Raycast = self.Shared.Raycast;
    FOVController = self.Controllers.FOVController;
    Maid = self.Shared.Maid;
end;

return CarController;

local MIN_STEER_ANGLE = 15;

local tonumber = tonumber;

local endInputState = Enum.UserInputState.End;

local FKeyCode = Enum.KeyCode.F;
local LKeyCode = Enum.KeyCode.L;
local QKeyCode = Enum.KeyCode.Q;

local tweenInfo1 = TweenInfo.new(0.11, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear, Enum.EasingDirection.Out);

local postSimulation = game:GetService('RunService').Heartbeat;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local ConvertSpeed;
local Map;
local CarRadar;

local SteerLeft = 0;
local SteerRight = 0;

local accelerating = false;
local braking = false;
local steerLeft = false;
local steerRight = false;

local mobileCarGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('MobileCarGUI');
local mobileMainFrame = mobileCarGUI.Frame;
local mobileAccelerateBtn = mobileMainFrame.AccelerateBtn;
local mobileBrakeBtn = mobileMainFrame.BrakeBtn;

local mobileSteerRightBtn = mobileMainFrame.SteerRightBtn;
