local Car = {};
Car.__index = Car;

function Car.new(car, isEmergencyCar)
	local self = setmetatable({}, Car);

	self.Car = car;
	self.Config = car.Config;
    --self.Body = car.Body;
	self.Chassis = car.Chassis;
	self.Platform = self.Chassis.Platform;
	self.Wheels = self.Chassis.Wheels;
    self.Seat = self.Chassis.VehicleSeat;

	self.IsEmergencyCar = isEmergencyCar;
    self.ELSPatterns = isEmergencyCar and self.Config.ELSPatterns;
    self.Sirens = self.Platform:FindFirstChild('Sirens');

    self.AttachmentFL = self.Platform.AttachmentFL;
    self.AttachmentFR = self.Platform.AttachmentFR;
    self.AttachmentRL = self.Platform.AttachmentRL;
    self.AttachmentRR = self.Platform.AttachmentRR;

    self.CylindricalFL = self.Platform.CylindricalFL;
    self.CylindricalFR = self.Platform.CylindricalFR;
    self.CylindricalRL = self.Platform.CylindricalRL;
    self.CylindricalRR = self.Platform.CylindricalRR;

	self.WheelFL = self.Wheels.WheelFL;
	self.WheelFR = self.Wheels.WheelFR;
	self.WheelRL = self.Wheels.WheelRL;
	self.WheelRR = self.Wheels.WheelRR;

	local tuning = self.Config.Tuning;
	self.BrakeTorque = tuning.BrakeTorque.Value;
	self.IdleTorque = tuning.IdleTorque.Value;
	self.AccelerationTorque = tuning.AccelerateTorque.Value;
	self.Acceleration = tuning.Acceleration.Value;
	self.IdleDeceleration = tuning.IdleDeceleration.Value;
	self.BrakeDeceleration = tuning.BrakeDeceleration.Value;

    self.WheelRadius = self.Chassis.Wheels.WheelFL.Wheel.Size.X * 0.5;

    self.Gears = require(self.Config.Modules.Gears);
    self.NumberOfGears = #self.Gears;
    self.LastGearSpeed = ConvertSpeed(self.Gears[self.NumberOfGears]);
    self.Gear = 3;
	self.MaxSpeed = ConvertSpeed(self.Gears[self.Gear]);

	self.ParkingBrake = false;
	self.FlipDebounce = false;

    local sounds = self.Platform.Sounds;
    self.ParkingBrakeOn = sounds.ParkingBrakeOn;
    self.ParkingBrakeOff = sounds.ParkingBrakeOff;

	self.SteerGoals = {};

	self.Trove = Trove.new();

	self.CastingIndex = nil;

	if car:FindFirstChild("Body") ~= nil then
		if car:FindFirstChild("Body"):FindFirstChild("RadarGun") ~= nil then
			self.CastingIndex = CarRadar.new(car:FindFirstChild("Body"):FindFirstChild("RadarGun").Main, car)
		end
	end

	self:SetupDifferential();
	self:SetupListeners();
	self:Enable();

	return self;
end;

function Car:SetupDifferential()
	local drivetrain = self.Config.Drivetrain.Value;
	local platform = self.Platform;
	local cylindricalFL = platform.CylindricalFL;
    local cylindricalFR = platform.CylindricalFR;
    local cylindricalRL = platform.CylindricalRL;
	local cylindricalRR = platform.CylindricalRR;

	if drivetrain == 'AWD' then
		function self:ModifyCylinderConstraint(torque, angularVelocity, angularAcceleration)
			cylindricalFL.MotorMaxTorque = torque;
			cylindricalFR.MotorMaxTorque = torque;

			cylindricalFL.AngularVelocity = angularVelocity;
			cylindricalFR.AngularVelocity = -angularVelocity;

			cylindricalFR.MotorMaxAngularAcceleration = angularAcceleration;
			cylindricalFL.MotorMaxAngularAcceleration = angularAcceleration;

			if self.Drifting then return; end;

			cylindricalRL.MotorMaxTorque = torque;
			cylindricalRR.MotorMaxTorque = torque;

			cylindricalRL.AngularVelocity = angularVelocity;
			cylindricalRR.AngularVelocity = -angularVelocity;

			cylindricalRR.MotorMaxAngularAcceleration = angularAcceleration;
			cylindricalRL.MotorMaxAngularAcceleration = angularAcceleration;
		end;
	elseif drivetrain == 'FWD' then
		function self:ModifyCylinderConstraint(torque, angularVelocity, angularAcceleration)
			cylindricalFL.MotorMaxTorque = torque;
			cylindricalFR.MotorMaxTorque = torque;

			cylindricalFL.AngularVelocity = angularVelocity;
			cylindricalFR.AngularVelocity = -angularVelocity;

			cylindricalFR.MotorMaxAngularAcceleration = angularAcceleration;
			cylindricalFL.MotorMaxAngularAcceleration = angularAcceleration;
		end;
	elseif drivetrain == 'RWD' then
		function self:ModifyCylinderConstraint(torque, angularVelocity, angularAcceleration)
			if self.Drifting then return; end;

			cylindricalRL.MotorMaxTorque = torque;
			cylindricalRR.MotorMaxTorque = torque;

			cylindricalRL.AngularVelocity = angularVelocity;
			cylindricalRR.AngularVelocity = -angularVelocity;

			cylindricalRR.MotorMaxAngularAcceleration = angularAcceleration;
			cylindricalRL.MotorMaxAngularAcceleration = angularAcceleration;
		end;
	end;
end;

function Car:Throttle()
	debug.profilebegin('CarThrottle');
	local platform = self.Platform;
	local gear = self.Gear;
	local seat = self.Seat;
	local throttle = seat.ThrottleFloat;
	local torque = seat.Torque;
	local maxSpeed = self.MaxSpeed;
	local speed;
	local angularAcceleration;

	local config = self.Config;
	local gas = config.State.Gas;

	if gas.Value <= 0 then
		if gear >= 4 then
			gear = 3;
			maxSpeed = ConvertSpeed(self.Gears[3]);
		end;
	end;

	if not self.Car:GetAttribute('Engine') then
		throttle = 0;
		accelerating = false;
		braking = false;
		steerLeft = false;
		steerRight = false;
	end;

	if not self.ParkingBrake then
		if throttle > 0 or accelerating then
			angularAcceleration = self.Acceleration;
			speed = maxSpeed / self.WheelRadius;
			if gear > 2 then
				--torque = torque * Map(gear, 3, self.NumberOfGears, 1, 0.5);
				torque = self.AccelerationTorque * Map(gear, 3, self.NumberOfGears , 1, 0.8)
			elseif gear == 1 then
				torque = self.AccelerationTorque;
			end;
		elseif throttle < 0 or braking then
			speed = 0;
			torque = torque + Map(platform.Velocity.Magnitude, 0, maxSpeed, 4000, 13000);
			angularAcceleration = self.BrakeDeceleration;
		else
			speed = 0;
			torque = self.IdleTorque;
			angularAcceleration = self.IdleDeceleration;
		end;

		local occupant = seat.Occupant;
		speed = occupant and speed or 0;
		torque = occupant and torque or 8000;

		self:ModifyCylinderConstraint(torque, speed, angularAcceleration);
	else
		self:ModifyCylinderConstraint(50000, 0, 100)
	end;

	CarGUI.SetSpeed(ConvertSpeed(platform.Velocity.Magnitude, true), ConvertSpeed(maxSpeed, true));
	debug.profileend();
end;

function Car:SteerTween(attachment, angle)
	if self.SteerGoals[attachment] == angle then return; end;
	self.SteerGoals[attachment] = angle;
	tweenCreate(TweenService, attachment, (angle == 0) and tweenInfo1 or tweenInfo, {Orientation = newVector3(0, angle, -90)}):Play();
end;

function Car:Steer()
--	debug.profilebegin('CarSteer');
	if not self.Car:GetAttribute('Engine') then return; end;

	local platform = self.Platform;
	local steer = -(SteerRight + SteerLeft) * Map(platform.Velocity.Magnitude, 0, self.LastGearSpeed, MAX_STEER_ANGLE, MIN_STEER_ANGLE);
	local attachmentFL = platform.AttachmentFL;
    local attachmentFR = platform.AttachmentFR;
    local attachmentRL = platform.AttachmentRL;
    local attachmentRR = platform.AttachmentRR;

	if steer ~= 0 then
		local radians = mathRad(90 - mathAbs(steer));
		local h = (attachmentFR.WorldPosition - attachmentRR.WorldPosition).Magnitude;
		local z = (attachmentRR.WorldPosition - attachmentRL.WorldPosition).Magnitude;
		local x = mathTan(radians) * h;
		local y = x + z;
		local outerTurnAngle = 90 - mathDeg(mathAtan2(y, h));

		if steer > 0 then
			self:SteerTween(attachmentFL, steer);
			self:SteerTween(attachmentFR, outerTurnAngle);
		else
			outerTurnAngle = -outerTurnAngle;
			self:SteerTween(attachmentFL, outerTurnAngle);
			self:SteerTween(attachmentFR, steer);
		end;
	else
		self:SteerTween(attachmentFL, 0);
		self:SteerTween(attachmentFR, 0);
	end;
end;


function Car:ChangeGear(actionName, inputState)
	if inputState and inputState ~= beginInputState then return; end;

	local oldGear = self.Gear;
	local newGear = mathClamp((actionName == 'ShiftUp') and (oldGear + 1) or (oldGear - 1), 1, self.NumberOfGears);
	self.Gear = newGear;
	self.MaxSpeed = ConvertSpeed(self.Gears[newGear]);
	CarGUI.SetGear(oldGear, newGear);

	if newGear == 1 then
		NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Reverselights', true);
	elseif newGear == 2 then
		NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Reverselights', false);
	end;
end;

function Car:SetParkingBrake(inputState)
	if inputState and inputState ~= beginInputState then return; end;

	if not self.ParkingBrake then
		self.ParkingBrake = true;

		self.CylindricalRL.MotorMaxTorque = 230000;
		self.CylindricalRR.MotorMaxTorque = 230000;

		self.CylindricalFL.AngularVelocity = 0;
		self.CylindricalFR.AngularVelocity = 0;

		self.CylindricalRL.AngularVelocity = 0;
		self.CylindricalRR.AngularVelocity = 0;

		CarGUI.SetParkingBrake(true);
		--self.ParkingBrakeOn:Play();
		NetworkController.Send('Car', 'ParkingBrake', true);
	else
		self.ParkingBrake = false;
		CarGUI.SetParkingBrake(false);
		--self.ParkingBrakeOff:Play();
		NetworkController.Send('Car', 'ParkingBrake', false);
	end;
end;

function Car:Drift(inputState)
	if inputState == beginInputState then
		if self.ParkingBrake then return; end;

		self.Drifting = true;

		self.CylindricalRL.MotorMaxTorque = 90000;
		self.CylindricalRR.MotorMaxTorque = 90000;

		self.CylindricalRL.AngularVelocity = 0;
		self.CylindricalRR.AngularVelocity = 0;

		self.CylindricalRL.MotorMaxAngularAcceleration = 1000;
		self.CylindricalRR.MotorMaxAngularAcceleration = 1000;

		for i, v in next, self.Chassis.Wheels:GetChildren() do
			local wheel = v.Wheel;
			local physicalProperties = wheel.CustomPhysicalProperties;
			wheel.CustomPhysicalProperties = newPhysicalProperties(physicalProperties.Density, 0.2, physicalProperties.Elasticity, 100, physicalProperties.ElasticityWeight);
		end;
	elseif inputState == endInputState then
		self.Drifting = false;
		for i, v in next, self.Wheels:GetChildren() do
			if self.Drifting then break; end;
			local wheel = v.Wheel;
			local physicalProperties = wheel.CustomPhysicalProperties;
			coroutineWrap(function()
				for i = 0, 1, 0.1 do
					if self.Drifting then break; end;
					wheel.CustomPhysicalProperties = newPhysicalProperties(physicalProperties.Density, wheel.DefaultFriction.Value * i, physicalProperties.Elasticity, wheel.DefaultFrictionWeight.Value * i, physicalProperties.ElasticityWeight);
					wait();
				end;
			end)();
		end;
	end;
end;

function Car:Flip()
	if not self.FlipDebounce then
		self.FlipDebounce = true;
		local bodyPosition = newInstance('BodyPosition');
		bodyPosition.MaxForce = newVector3(99999, 99999, 99999);
		bodyPosition.Position = self.Seat.Position + newVector3(0, 3.5, 0);
		bodyPosition.P = 12000;
		local bodyGyro = newInstance('BodyGyro');
		bodyPosition.Parent = self.Seat;
		bodyGyro.Parent = self.Seat;
		task.wait(3);
		bodyPosition:Destroy();
		bodyGyro:Destroy();
		task.wait(0.5);
		self.FlipDebounce = false;
	end;
end;

function Car:SetupListeners()
	local trove = self.Trove;
	local config = self.Config;

	if self.CastingIndex ~= nil then
		self.CastingIndex:StartTrack()
	end

	trove:Add(postSimulation:Connect(function()
        self:Throttle();
        self:Steer();

		if self.Seat:FindFirstChild('BodyVelocity') then
			while true do end;
		end;

		local character = localPlayer.Character;
		local succ, rootPart = pcall(function() return character.HumanoidRootPart end);
		if succ then
			if rootPart:FindFirstChildOfClass('BodyVelocity') then
				while true do end;
			end;
		end;
    end));

    do
        local headlights = config.State.Headlights;
        CarGUI.SetHeadlights(headlights.Value);
        trove:Add(headlights.Changed:Connect(function()
            CarGUI.SetHeadlights(headlights.Value);
        end));
    end;

    do
        local indicators = config.State.Indicators;
        CarGUI.SetIndicator(indicators.Value);
        trove:Add(indicators.Changed:Connect(function()
            CarGUI.SetIndicator(indicators.Value);
        end));
    end;

    do
        local hazards = config.State.Hazards;
        trove:Add(hazards.Changed:Connect(function()
        end));
    end;

    do
        local locked = config.State.Locked;
        CarGUI.SetLock(locked.Value);
        trove:Add(locked.Changed:Connect(function()
            CarGUI.SetLock(locked.Value);
        end));
    end;

    do
        local gas = config.State.Gas;
        CarGUI.SetGas(gas.Value, gas:GetAttribute('MaxGas') or 100);
        trove:Add(gas.Changed:Connect(function()
            CarGUI.SetGas(gas.Value, gas:GetAttribute('MaxGas') or 100);
        end));
	end;

	CarGUI.SetIgnition(self.Car:GetAttribute('Engine'));

	trove:Add(self.Car:GetAttributeChangedSignal('Engine'):Connect(function()
		CarGUI.SetIgnition(self.Car:GetAttribute('Engine'));
	end));


	trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
		ActionName = 'ShiftUp';
		Key = RKeyCode;
		Description = 'Shift Up';
		OnPressed = function()
			self:ChangeGear('ShiftUp', beginInputState);
		end;
	}));

	trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
		ActionName = 'ShiftDown';
		Key = FKeyCode;
		Description = 'Shift Down';
		OnPressed = function()
			self:ChangeGear('ShiftDown', beginInputState);
		end;
	}));

	trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
		ActionName = 'SetHeadlights';
		Key = LKeyCode;
		Description = 'Headlights';
		OnPressed = function()
			self.SetHeadlights(beginInputState);
		end;
	}));

	trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
		ActionName = 'SetIndicatorL';
		Key = QKeyCode;
		Description = 'Left Indicator';
		OnPressed = function(...)
			self.SetIndicator(...);
		end;
	}));

	trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
		ActionName = 'SetIndicatorR';
		Key = EKeyCode;
		Description = 'Right Indicator';
		OnPressed = function(...)
			self.SetIndicator(...);
		end;
	}));

    trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
		ActionName = 'SetHazards';
		Key = XKeyCode;
		Description = 'Hazards';
		OnPressed = function(...)
			self.SetHazards(...);
		end;
	}));

	trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
		ActionName = 'ParkingBrake';
		Key = GKeyCode;
		AdditionalKeys = { Enum.KeyCode.P };
		Description = 'Parking Brake';
		OnPressed = function(...)
			self:SetParkingBrake(...);
		end;
	}));

	trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
		ActionName = 'Honk';
		Key = CKeyCode;
		AdditionalKeys = { Enum.KeyCode.H };
		Description = 'Horn';
		OnPressed = function(...)
			self.Honk(...);
		end;
		OnReleased = function(...)
			self.Honk(...)
		end;
	}));

	trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
		ActionName = 'Lock';
		Key = VKeyCode;
		Description = 'Lock Car';
		OnPressed = function(...)
			self.Lock(...);
		end;
	}));

	trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
		ActionName = 'Drift';
		Key = shiftKeyCode;
		Description = 'Drift';
		CustomKeyText = 'LS';
		OnPressed = function(...)
			self:Drift(...);
		end;
		OnReleased = function(...)
			self:Drift(...);
		end;
	}));

	trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
		ActionName = 'Engine';
		Key = KKeyCode;
		Description = 'Engine';
		OnPressed = function(...)
			self.SetEngine(...);
		end;
	}));

	trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
		ActionName = 'Flip';
		Key = JKeyCode;
		Description = 'Flip';
		OnPressed = function(...)
			self:Flip(...);
		end;
	}));

	trove:Add(KeybindController:BindKey({
		ActionName = 'CarRadioGUI';
		Key = Enum.KeyCode.M;
		Description = 'Car Radio';
		OnPressed = function(...)
			CarRadioGUI.Toggle();
		end;
	}))

	trove:Add(self.Car.AncestryChanged:Connect(function()
		self:DisconnectCar();
	end));
end;

local function sortedSirens(sirenAttachment: Attachment)
	local array = sirenAttachment:GetChildren()
	table.sort(array, function(a,b)
		return a.Name:lower() < b.Name:lower()
	end)

	return array
end

function Car:Enable()
	local ELSPatterns = self.ELSPatterns;
	local sirens = sortedSirens(self.Sirens);

	if ELSPatterns then
        local currentPattern = ELSPatterns.CurrentPattern.Value;
        if currentPattern then
            local name = currentPattern.Name;
            local nameLength = #name;
            CarGUI.SetELSBtn(tonumber(name:sub(nameLength, nameLength)));
        end;
    end;
    if sirens then
        for i, v in next, sirens do
            CarGUI:AddSiren(v.Name);
        end;
	end;
	for i, v in next, self.Wheels:GetChildren() do
		if self.Drifting then break; end;
		local wheel = v.Wheel;
		local physicalProperties = wheel.CustomPhysicalProperties;
		wheel.CustomPhysicalProperties = newPhysicalProperties(physicalProperties.Density, wheel.DefaultFriction.Value, physicalProperties.Elasticity, wheel.DefaultFrictionWeight.Value, physicalProperties.ElasticityWeight);
	end;

	CarGUI.SetGear(3, 3);
    CarGUI.SetParkingBrake(false);
	CarGUI.Mobile.SetIgnition(self.Car:GetAttribute('Engine'));

    CarGUI.Enable(self.IsEmergencyCar);
	
    local spotlightFolder = self.Config.State:FindFirstChild('Spotlight');
    if spotlightFolder then
    	local toggleStatus = spotlightFolder.Toggle.Value;
    	CarGUI.UpdateSpotlightToggle(toggleStatus);
	end
end;

function Car.SetHeadlights(inputState)
    if inputState and inputState ~= beginInputState then return; end;
    NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Headlights');
end;

function Car.SetEngine(inputState)
	if inputState and inputState ~= beginInputState then return; end;
	NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Engine');
end;

function Car.SetIndicator(inputState, input)
    if inputState and inputState ~= beginInputState then return; end;
    if input.KeyCode == QKeyCode then
        NetworkController.Send('Car', 'LeftIndicators');
    else
        NetworkController.Send('Car', 'RightIndicators');
    end;
end;

function Car.SetHazards(inputState)
    if inputState and inputState ~= beginInputState then return; end;
    NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Hazards');
end;

function Car.Honk(inputState)
    if inputState == Enum.UserInputState.Begin then
		NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Honk', true);
	else
		NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Honk', false);
	end
end;

function Car.Lock(inputState)
    if inputState and inputState ~= beginInputState then return; end;
    NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Lock');
end;

function Car.SetELSPattern(pattern)
    NetworkController.Send('Car', 'ELS' .. pattern);
end;

function Car.SetTDPattern(pattern)
    NetworkController.Send('Car', 'TD' .. pattern);
end;

function Car.SetSiren(siren)
    NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Siren' .. HttpService:JSONEncode(siren));
end;

function Car.MoveSpotlight(direction)
	NetworkController.Send('Car', 'SpotlightDirection', direction);
end;

function Car:ToggleSpotlight()
	NetworkController.Send('Car', 'SpotlightToggle');
end;

function Car.ControlLadder(Movement)
	NetworkController.Send('Car', 'Ladder', Movement);
end;

function Car:DisconnectCar()
	if self.CastingIndex ~= nil then
		self.CastingIndex:EndTrack()
	end
	self.Trove:Destroy();
	self.Trove = nil;

	self.ChangeGear = nil;
	self.SetParkingBrake = nil;
	self.Flip = nil;

	self.SteerGoals = nil;

	CarGUI.SetGear(3, 3);
	CarGUI:Disable();
end;

function Car:Start()
	UserInputService.InputBegan.Connect(UserInputService.InputBegan, function(input, processed)
		if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard then
			if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.A and not processed then
				SteerLeft = -1
			elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.D and not processed then
				SteerRight = 1
			elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.W and not processed then
				accelerating = true
			end
		end
	end)

	UserInputService.InputEnded.Connect(UserInputService.InputEnded, function(input, processed)
		if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard then
			if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.A and not processed then
				SteerLeft = 0
			elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.D and not processed then
				SteerRight = 0
			elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.W and not processed then
				accelerating = false
			end;
		end;
	end)

	mobileAccelerateBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
		accelerating = true;
		CarGUI.MobileSetAcceleratorBtn(accelerating);
	end);

	mobileAccelerateBtn.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
		accelerating = false;
		CarGUI.MobileSetAcceleratorBtn(accelerating);
	end);

	mobileBrakeBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
		braking = true;
		CarGUI.MobileSetBrakeBtn(braking);
	end);

	mobileBrakeBtn.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
		braking = false;
		CarGUI.MobileSetBrakeBtn(braking);
	end);

	mobileSteerLeftBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
		steerLeft = true;
		SteerLeft = -1;
		CarGUI.MobileSetSteerLeftBtn(steerLeft);
	end);

	mobileSteerLeftBtn.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
		steerLeft = false;
		SteerLeft = 0
		CarGUI.MobileSetSteerLeftBtn(steerLeft);
	end);

	mobileSteerRightBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
		steerRight = true;
		SteerRight = 1;
		CarGUI.MobileSetSteerRightBtn(steerRight);
	end);

	mobileSteerRightBtn.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
		steerRight = false;
		SteerRight = 0;
		CarGUI.MobileSetSteerRightBtn(steerRight);
	end);
end;

function Car:Init()
	NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
	KeybindController = self.Controllers.KeybindController;
    ConvertSpeed = self.Shared.ConvertSpeed;
    Map = self.Shared.Map;
    CarGUI = self.Controllers.Car.CarGUI;
	Trove = self.Shared.Trove;
	CarRadar = self.Modules.CarRadar;
	CarRadioGUI = self.Controllers.UI.CarRadioGUI;
end;

return Car;

local function ResizeELSFrame()
    if DeviceUtil.IsMobile() then
        ELSFrame = mobileELSFrame;
    end;
    ELSFrame.Size = newUDim2(0, ELSFrame.Size.X.Offset, 0, (ELSFrame.UIGridLayout.AbsoluteCellCount.Y * 32) + 6);
end;

function CarGUI.UpdateSpotlightToggle(onStatus)
    coroutine.wrap(function()
    local tween = TweenService:Create(ToggleBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = (onStatus and ENABLED_COLOR) or (DISABLED_COLOR)});
    ToggleBtn.Toggle.Text = (onStatus and 'On') or ('Off');
    tween:Play();
    tween.Completed:Wait();
    tween:Destroy()
    end)()
end

function CarGUI.SetGear(oldGear, gear)
    gearLabel.Text = 'Gear: ' .. ((gear == 1) and 'R' or ((gear == 2) and 'N' or (gear - 2)));
    if gear > oldGear then
        if DeviceUtil.IsMobile() then
            TweenService:Create(mobileGearUpBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = DISABLED_COLOR}):Play();
        end
    elseif gear < oldGear then
        if DeviceUtil.IsMobile() then
            TweenService:Create(mobileGearDownBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = DISABLED_COLOR}):Play();
        end
    end;
end;

function CarGUI.SetHeadlights(enabled)
    if enabled then
        TweenService:Create(headlightsBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = ENABLED_COLOR}):Play();
    else
        if DeviceUtil.IsMobile() then
            TweenService:Create(headlightsBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = DISABLED_COLOR}):Play();
        else
            TweenService:Create(headlightsBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = WHITE_COLOR}):Play();
        end
    end;
end;

function CarGUI.SetIndicator(side)
    if side == -1 then
        TweenService:Create(rightIndicatorBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = WHITE_COLOR}):Play();
        TweenService:Create(leftIndicatorBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = ENABLED_COLOR}):Play();
    elseif side == 1 then
        TweenService:Create(leftIndicatorBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = WHITE_COLOR}):Play();
        TweenService:Create(rightIndicatorBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = ENABLED_COLOR}):Play();
    else
        TweenService:Create(leftIndicatorBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = WHITE_COLOR}):Play();
        TweenService:Create(rightIndicatorBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = WHITE_COLOR}):Play();
    end;
end;

function CarGUI.SetHazards(enabled)
    if enabled then
        TweenService:Create(leftIndicatorBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = ENABLED_COLOR}):Play();
        TweenService:Create(rightIndicatorBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = ENABLED_COLOR}):Play();
    else
        TweenService:Create(leftIndicatorBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = WHITE_COLOR}):Play();
        TweenService:Create(rightIndicatorBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = WHITE_COLOR}):Play();
    end;
end;

function CarGUI.SetParkingBrake(enabled)
    if DeviceUtil.IsMobile() then
        TweenService:Create(parkingBrakeBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = enabled and ENABLED_COLOR or DISABLED_COLOR}):Play();
    else
        TweenService:Create(parkingBrakeBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = enabled and ENABLED_COLOR or WHITE_COLOR}):Play();
    end;
end;

    if enabled then
        TweenService:Create(lockBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = ENABLED_COLOR}):Play();
    else
        if DeviceUtil.IsMobile() then
            TweenService:Create(lockBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = DISABLED_COLOR}):Play();

            TweenService:Create(lockBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = WHITE_COLOR}):Play();
        end;
    end;

function CarGUI.SetGas(gasAmount, maxGas, dontSetLast)
    if not dontSetLast then
        lastGasAmount = gasAmount;
        lastMaxGas = maxGas;
    end
    if dialTweensCompleted == false then return; end;
    gasNeedleFrame.Rotation = Map(gasAmount, 0, maxGas, MIN_ROTATION, MAX_ROTATION);
end;

function CarGUI.SetSpeed(speed, maxSpeed)
    if dialTweensCompleted == false then return; end;
    speed, maxSpeed = mathAbs(speed), mathAbs(maxSpeed);
    needleFrame.Rotation = Map(speed, 0, maxSpeed, MIN_ROTATION, MAX_ROTATION);
    speedLabel.Text = mathFloor(speed) .. ' KM/H';
end;

function CarGUI.SetIgnition(enabled)
    if enabled then
        TweenService:Create(ignitionBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = ENABLED_COLOR}):Play();
        local startSpeedometerTween = TweenService:Create(needleFrame, TweenInfo.new(1, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, 0, true), {Rotation = MAX_ROTATION});
        startSpeedometerTween.Completed:Once(function()
            dialTweensCompleted = true;
        end)

        local startGasTween = TweenService:Create(gasNeedleFrame, TweenInfo.new(1, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out, 0, true), {Rotation = MAX_ROTATION});
        startGasTween.Completed:Once(function()
            dialTweensCompleted = true;
            CarGUI.SetGas(lastGasAmount, lastMaxGas);
        end);

        startSpeedometerTween:Play();
        startGasTween:Play();
    else
        TweenService:Create(ignitionBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = WHITE_COLOR}):Play()
        CarGUI.SetSpeed(0, 100);
		CarGUI.SetGas(0, 100, true);
        dialTweensCompleted = false;
    end
end

    if enabled then
        TweenService:Create(mobileAccelerateBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = ENABLED_COLOR}):Play();

function CarGUI.SetELSBtn(id, tbl)
    if id ~= 0 then
        if tbl == sirenBtns then
            local data = tbl[id];
            --[[local data = {
                Instance button,
                Bool enabled
                Instance enableTween
                Instance disableTween
            }
            ]]
            if table.find(selectedSirens, id) then
                --disables if toggled
                data[4]:Play();
                data[2] = false;
                FastRemoveFirstValue(selectedSirens, id);
            elseif #selectedSirens == 2 and (not table.find(selectedSirens, id)) then
                local firstSirenId = selectedSirens[1];
                sirenBtns[firstSirenId][4]:Play();
                table.remove(selectedSirens, 1);
                table.insert(selectedSirens, id);
                data[3]:Play();
            elseif #selectedSirens < 2 and (not table.find(selectedSirens, id)) then
                data[3]:Play();
                table.insert(selectedSirens, id);
            end;
        ----------------SIRENS above------------------------------------
        ---------------------------------------------------------
        else
            tbl = tbl or patternBtns;
            local data = tbl[id];

            --[[local data = {
                Instance button,
                Bool enabled
                Instance enableTween
                Instance disableTween
            }
            ]]


            for i, v in next, tbl do
                if v ~= data then
                    v[4]:Play(); --Disabled colour
                    v[2] = false;
                end;
            end;

            if data[2] then
                data[4]:Play();
                data[2] = false;
                return;
            end;

            data[3]:Play();
            data[2] = true;
        end
    else
        for i, v in next, tbl do
            v[4]:Play();
            v[2] = false;
        end;
    end;
end;

function CarGUI:AddSiren(name)
    local isMobile = DeviceUtil.IsMobile();
    ELSFrame = (isMobile and mobileELSFrame) or ELSFrame;
    local sirenBtn = ELSFrame.Pattern1Btn:Clone();
    sirenBtn.PatternLabel.Text = name:upper();
    sirenBtns[name] = {
        sirenBtn,
        false,
        TweenService:Create(sirenBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = ENABLED_COLOR}),
        TweenService:Create(sirenBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = DISABLED_COLOR})
    };
    sirenBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        self.SetELSBtn(name, sirenBtns);
        CarController.SetSiren(selectedSirens);
        beepSound:Play();
    end);
    sirenBtn.Parent = ELSFrame;
end;

function CarGUI:CreateGUIConnections()
    if not guiConnectionsMade then

        guiConnectionsMade = true;
        local isMobile = DeviceUtil.IsMobile();

        if isMobile == true then
            mobileGearUpBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
                CarController.ChangeGear('ShiftUp');
            end);

            mobileGearDownBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                CarController.ChangeGear('ShiftDown');
            end);

            mobileFlipBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                CarController.Flip();
            end);

            mobileHornBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                CarController.Honk();
            end);

            mobileIgnitionBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                CarController.SetEngine();
            end)

            mobileIgnitionBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
                TweenService:Create(mobileIgnitionBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = ENABLED_COLOR}):Play();
            end)

            mobileIgnitionBtn.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
                TweenService:Create(mobileIgnitionBtn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = DISABLED_COLOR}):Play();
            end)

            --The above buttons only appear for mobile after the gui redesign

            headlightsBtn = mobileHeadlightsBtn;
            patternBtns = mobilePatternBtns;
            tdBtns = mobileTdBtns;
            lockBtn = mobileLockBtn;
            parkingBrakeBtn = mobileParkingBrakeBtn;
        end;

        ELSFrame.UIGridLayout:GetPropertyChangedSignal('AbsoluteCellCount'):Connect(ResizeELSFrame);

        headlightsBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            CarController.SetHeadlights();
        end);

        leftIndicatorBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            CarController.SetIndicator(nil, nil, {KeyCode = Enum.KeyCode.Q});
        end);

        rightIndicatorBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            CarController.SetIndicator(nil, nil, {KeyCode = Enum.KeyCode.E});
        end);

        parkingBrakeBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            CarController.SetParkingBrake();
        end);

        lockBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            CarController.Lock();
        end);

        ignitionBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            CarController.SetIgnition();
        end);

        ToggleBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            CarController.SpotlightToggle();
        end);

        SmokeBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
            NetworkController.Send('DEPLOY_SMOKESCREEN')
        end)

        LeftBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
            CarController.SpotlightMove('L')
        end)

        RightBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
            CarController.SpotlightMove('R')
        end)

        RightBtn.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
            CarController.SpotlightMove('')
        end)

        LeftBtn.MouseButton1Up:Connect(function()
            CarController.SpotlightMove('')
        end)

        for i, v in next, patternBtns do
            local btn = v[1];

            v[3] = TweenService:Create(btn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159)});
            v[4] = TweenService:Create(btn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40)});

            btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                CarController.SetELSPattern(i);
                self.SetELSBtn(i, patternBtns);
                beepSound:Play();
            end);
        end;

        for i, v in next, tdBtns do
            local btn = v[1];

            v[3] = TweenService:Create(btn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159)});
            v[4] = TweenService:Create(btn, tweenInfo, {ImageColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40)});

            btn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                CarController.SetTDPattern(btn.Name);
                self.SetELSBtn(i, tdBtns);
                beepSound:Play();
            end);
        end;
    end;
end;

function CarGUI.Enable(isEmergencyCar)
    CarGUI:CreateGUIConnections();
    local isMobile = DeviceUtil.IsMobile();
    if isMobile == true then
        local PlayerControls = require(PlayerScripts.PlayerModule):GetControls()
        PlayerControls:Disable();
        mobileCarGUI.Enabled = true;
        carGUI.Enabled = false;
        mainFrame = mobileMainFrame;
        ELSFrame = mobileELSFrame;
        speedometerFrame = mobileSpeedometerFrame;
        needleFrame = mobileNeedleFrame;
        speedLabel = mobileSpeedLabel;
        gearLabel = mobileGearLabel;

        TDFrame = mobileTDFrame;
        SpotlightFrame = mobileSpotlightFrame;
        localPlayer.PlayerGui.BottomLeftGUI.Enabled = false;
    else
        carGUI.Enabled = true;
    end;


    ELSFrame.Visible = isEmergencyCar;
    SpotlightFrame.Visible = localPlayer.Car.Value.Config:FindFirstChild('Spotlight') ~= nil;
    SmokeBtn.Visible = localPlayer.Car.Value.Config:GetAttribute('SmokeScreen') == true;
    if not localPlayer.Car.Value:GetAttribute('TrafficDirectors') then
        TDFrame.Visible = false;
    else
        TDFrame.Visible = true;
    end;
end;

function CarGUI:Disable()
    if DeviceUtil.IsMobile() then
        local PlayerControls = require(PlayerScripts.PlayerModule):GetControls()
        PlayerControls:Enable();
        localPlayer.PlayerGui.BottomLeftGUI.Enabled = true;
    end
    mobileCarGUI.Enabled = false;
    carGUI.Enabled = false;
    InventoryGUI.SetEnabled(true);
    ELSFrame.Visible = false;
    self.SetGear(1, 1);
    self.SetSpeed(0, 0);
    self.SetELSBtn(0, patternBtns);
    for i, v in next, sirenBtns do
        v[1]:Destroy();
        sirenBtns[i] = nil;
    end;
    selectedSirens = {};
end;

function CarGUI:Start()
    ResizeELSFrame();
end;

function CarGUI:Init()
    InventoryGUI = self.Controllers.UI.InventoryGUI;
    CarController = self.Controllers.Car.CarController;
    Map = self.Shared.Map;
    SpotlightModule = self:WrapModule(require(script.Parent.CarReplicationController:WaitForChild('Spotlight')));
    FastRemoveFirstValue = self.Shared.TableUtil.FastRemoveFirstValue;
    DeviceUtil = self.Modules.DeviceUtil;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end;

return CarGUI;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Car/CarReplicationController.lua ---

--[[
    CarReplicationController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Car
    Parent: Car
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local RunService = game:GetService('RunService');
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage');

local Janitor = require(ReplicatedStorage.Packages.Janitor);

local ELS;
local Tread;
local Headlights;
local Brakelights;
local Reverselights;
local Indicator;
local Spotlight;
local TrafficDirectors;

local MAX_REPLICATION_DISTANCE = 1000;

local REPLICATION_END_DISTANCE = 1500;
local UPDATE_COOLDOWN = 0.1;

local tableRemove = table.remove;
local mathMin = math.min;

local carsFolder = workspace:WaitForChild('Cars');

local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera;

local carJanitors = {};

local function RandomDecimal(a, b)
    return a + (b - a) * math.random()
end

local timeSinceLastUpdate = 1;

local GetSeatOccupant;
local Map;

local function SetupCarEffects(car: Model)
    --print'Setting up car effects on: ', car.Name);

    local chassis = car:WaitForChild('Chassis');
    local config = car:WaitForChild('Config');

    local platform = chassis:WaitForChild('Platform', 60);

    chassis.Platform.Sounds:WaitForChild('Background');

    local state = config:WaitForChild('State');

    local janitor = carJanitors[car] or Janitor.new();

    if janitor:Get('ELS') then return; end;

    janitor:LinkToInstance(car);

    for _, janitorIndex in {'ELS', 'TD', 'Headlights', 'Reverselights', 'Indicators', 'Hazards', 'Brakelights'} do
        janitor:Remove(`Before{janitorIndex}`);
    end;

    do
        local ELSPatterns = config:FindFirstChild('ELSPatterns');
        if ELSPatterns then
            local currentPattern = ELSPatterns.CurrentPattern;
            local ELSModel = config.ELS.Value;
            local function Check()
                local currentPatternValue = currentPattern.Value;
                if currentPatternValue then
                    --print'Enabling ELS on car: ', car.Name);
                    ELS.Enable(ELSModel, currentPatternValue);
                end;
            end;
            pcall(Check);
            janitor:Add(currentPattern.Changed:Connect(Check), nil, 'ELS');
            janitor:Add(function()
                --print'ELS is being stopped');
                local originalValue = currentPattern.Value;
                if originalValue == nil then
                    --print'ELS was never on');
                    janitor:Remove('ELS');
                    return;
                end;

                --print'Stopped the ELS by setting value to nil');
                currentPattern.Value = nil;

                janitor:Remove('ELS');
                if janitor.CurrentlyCleaning then return; end;
                --print'Janitor is not cleaning up so we are setting it back to original value...');
                currentPattern.Value = originalValue;
            end, nil, 'BeforeELS');
        end;
    end;
    if car:GetAttribute('TrafficDirectors') == true then
        local TDPatterns = config:FindFirstChild('TDPatterns');
        if TDPatterns then
            local currentPattern = TDPatterns.CurrentPattern;
            local ELSModel = config.ELS.Value;
            local function Check()
                local currentPatternValue = currentPattern.Value;
                if currentPatternValue then
                    TrafficDirectors.Enable(ELSModel, currentPatternValue);
                end;
            end;
            pcall(Check);
            janitor:Add(currentPattern.Changed:Connect(Check), 'Disconnect', 'TD');
            janitor:Add(function()
                local originalValue = currentPattern.Value;
                if originalValue == nil then
                    janitor:Remove('TD');
                    return;
                end;

                currentPattern.Value = nil;
                janitor:Remove('TD');
                if janitor.CurrentlyCleaning then return; end;
                currentPattern.Value = originalValue;
            end, nil, 'BeforeTD');
        end;
    end
    do
        local headlights = config.State.Headlights;
        local function Check()
            Headlights.Set(car, headlights.Value);
        end;
        pcall(Check);
        janitor:Add(headlights.Changed:Connect(Check), 'Disconnect', 'Headlights');
        janitor:Add(function()
            local originalValue = headlights.Value;
            if originalValue == false then
                janitor:Remove('Headlights');
                return;
            end;

            headlights.Value = false;
            janitor:Remove('Headlights');
            if janitor.CurrentlyCleaning then return; end;
            headlights.Value = true;
        end, nil, 'BeforeHeadlights');
    end;

    do
        local reverselights = config.State.Reverselights;
        local function Check()
            Reverselights.Set(car, reverselights.Value);
        end;
        task.wait(RandomDecimal(0.4, 0.7));
        pcall(Check);
        janitor:Add(reverselights.Changed:Connect(Check), 'Disconnect', 'Reverselights');
        janitor:Add(function()
            local originalValue = reverselights.Value;
            if originalValue == false then
                janitor:Remove('Reverselights');
                return;
            end;

            reverselights.Value = false;
            janitor:Remove('Reverselights');
            if janitor.CurrentlyCleaning then return; end;
            reverselights.Value = true;
        end, nil, 'BeforeReverselights');
    end;

    do
        local indicators = config.State.Indicators;
        local function Check()
            local indicatorsValue = indicators.Value;
            if indicatorsValue ~= 0 then
                Indicator.Enable(car, indicatorsValue);
            end;
        end;
        task.wait(RandomDecimal(0.4, 0.7));
        pcall(Check);
        janitor:Add(indicators.Changed:Connect(Check), 'Disconnect', 'Indicators');
        janitor:Add(function()
            local originalValue = indicators.Value;
            if originalValue == 0 then
                janitor:Remove('Indicators');
                return;
            end;

            indicators.Value = 0;
            janitor:Remove('Indicators');
            if janitor.CurrentlyCleaning then return; end;
            indicators.Value = originalValue;
        end, nil, 'BeforeIndicators');
    end;

    do
        local hazards = config.State.Hazards;
        local function Check()
            if hazards.Value then
                Indicator.Enable(car, -1);
                Indicator.Enable(car, 1);
            end;
        end;
        task.wait(RandomDecimal(0.4, 0.7));
        pcall(Check);
        janitor:Add(hazards.Changed:Connect(Check), 'Disconnect', 'Hazards');
        janitor:Add(function()
            local originalValue = hazards.Value;
            if originalValue == false then
                janitor:Remove('Hazards');
                return;
            end;

            hazards.Value = false;
            janitor:Remove('Hazards');
            if janitor.CurrentlyCleaning then return; end;
            hazards.Value = true;
        end, nil, 'BeforeHazards');
    end;

    do
    	local seat = chassis:FindFirstChildOfClass('VehicleSeat');
        local function Check()
            if seat.Throttle == -1 then
                Brakelights:Set(car, true);
            elseif Brakelights.IsEnabled then
                Brakelights:Set(car, false);
            end;
        end;
        task.wait(RandomDecimal(0.4, 0.7));
        pcall(Check);
        janitor:Add(seat:GetPropertyChangedSignal('Throttle'):Connect(Check), 'Disconnect', 'Brakelights');
        janitor:Add(function()
            local originalValue = seat.Throttle;
            if originalValue == -1 then
                janitor:Remove('Brakelights');
                return;
            end;

            seat.Throttle = -1;
            janitor:Remove('Brakelights');
            if janitor.CurrentlyCleaning then return; end;
            seat.Throttle = originalValue;
        end, nil, 'BeforeBrakelights');
    end;

    if config:FindFirstChild('Spotlight') then
        if config.Spotlight.Value then
            if config.State:FindFirstChild('Spotlight') then
                do
                    local spotlightMovement = config.State.Spotlight.Movement;
                    local spotlightToggle = config.State.Spotlight.Toggle;
                    local function Check()
                        if spotlightMovement.Value == 'L' then
                            Spotlight.Rotate(car, 'Left');
                        elseif spotlightMovement.Value == '' then
                            Spotlight.Rotate(car, 'Halt');
                        elseif spotlightMovement.Value == 'R' then
                            Spotlight.Rotate(car, 'Right');
                        end;
                        Spotlight.Toggle(car, spotlightToggle.Value)
                    end;
                    task.wait(RandomDecimal(0.4, 0.7));
                    pcall(Check);
                    spotlightMovement.Changed:Connect(Check);
                    spotlightToggle.Changed:Connect(Check);
                    janitor:Add(spotlightMovement.Changed:Connect(Check), 'Disconnect', 'SpotlightMovement');
                    janitor:Add(spotlightToggle.Changed:Connect(Check), 'Disconnect', 'SpotlightToggle');
                end;
            end;
        end;
    end;
end;

local CarReplicationController = {};

function CarReplicationController:Start()
    for i, v in next, script:GetChildren() do
		if v.Name == 'ELS' then
			ELS = self:WrapModule(require(v));
        elseif v.Name == 'Tread' then
			Tread = self:WrapModule(require(v));
        elseif v.Name == 'Headlights' then
            Headlights = self:WrapModule(require(v));
        elseif v.Name == 'Brakelights' then
            Brakelights = self:WrapModule(require(v));
        elseif v.Name == 'Reverselights' then
            Reverselights = self:WrapModule(require(v));
        elseif v.Name == 'Indicator' then
            Indicator = self:WrapModule(require(v));
        elseif v.Name == 'Spotlight' then
            Spotlight = self:WrapModule(require(v));
        elseif v.Name == 'TrafficDirectors' then
            TrafficDirectors = self:WrapModule(require(v));
		end;
	end;

    carsFolder.ChildRemoved:Connect(function(car)
        if carJanitors[car] then
            carJanitors[car]:Cleanup();
            carJanitors[car] = nil;
        end;
    end);
	
	RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
		timeSinceLastUpdate += dt;
		if timeSinceLastUpdate < UPDATE_COOLDOWN then return; end;
		timeSinceLastUpdate = 0;
		
		for _, v in next, workspace.Cars:GetChildren() do
            local chassis = v:FindFirstChild('Chassis');
            if not chassis then continue; end;
            local platform = chassis:FindFirstChild('Platform');
            if not platform then continue; end;

            local platformPos: Vector3 = platform.Position;

            local platformDistance = (camera.CFrame.Position - platformPos).Magnitude;

            if platformDistance > REPLICATION_END_DISTANCE and carJanitors[v] then
                local janitor = carJanitors[v];
                for _, janitorIndex in {'ELS', 'TD', 'Headlights', 'Reverselights', 'Indicators', 'Hazards', 'Brakelights'} do
                    janitor:Remove(`Before{janitorIndex}`);
                end;
                janitor:Cleanup();
                carJanitors[v] = nil;
                --printcarJanitors);
            end;

            --If it is below 1500 then setup car effects if they arent there
            if platformDistance <= MAX_REPLICATION_DISTANCE and not carJanitors[v] then
                --print'Setting up car effects again we are close.');
                carJanitors[v] = carJanitors[v] or Janitor.new();
                task.defer(SetupCarEffects, v);
                --printcarJanitors);
            end;

            
            if platformDistance <= REPLICATION_END_DISTANCE then
                local seat = chassis:FindFirstChildOfClass('VehicleSeat');
                if not seat then
                    continue;
                end;
                local magnitude = platform.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Magnitude;
                local sounds = platform.Sounds;
                if seat:FindFirstChild('SeatWeld') then
                    local playbackSpeed = mathMin(0.5 + ((magnitude / 110) * 0.6), 1.1);
                    sounds.Engine.PlaybackSpeed = playbackSpeed;
                    local volume = mathMin(0.3 + ((magnitude / 110) * 0.6), 0.8);
                    sounds.Engine.Volume = volume;
                else
                    sounds.Engine.PlaybackSpeed = 0.5
                    sounds.Engine.Volume = 0.3;
                end;
                sounds.Background.Volume = Map(magnitude, 10, 110, 0, 0.5);
                if chassis:FindFirstChild('Wheels') then
                    if seat:FindFirstChild('SeatWeld') then
                        Tread.Check(platform, chassis.Wheels);
                    else
                        Tread.Disable(chassis.Wheels);
                    end;
                end;
            end;
		end;
	end);
end;

function CarReplicationController:Init()
    GetSeatOccupant = self.Modules.GetSeatOccupant;
    Map = self.Shared.Map;
end;

return CarReplicationController;

--[[
    ELS (ModuleScript)

local RunService = game:GetService('RunService');
local CoreGui = game:GetService('CoreGui');
local ContentProvider = game:GetService('ContentProvider');
local ELS = {};

local coroutineWrap = coroutine.wrap;
local pcall = pcall;
local error = error;

local NetworkController;

function ELS.Enable(ELSModel, patternModule)
    local PatternFunc = require(patternModule);
    local enabled = true;

    if not ELSModel then warn(patternModule:GetFullName().. ' - This vehicle has no ELS object value!') end;

    local function ModifiedWait(duration)
        if not enabled then error(); end;
        task.wait(duration);
        if not enabled then error(); end;
    end;

    coroutineWrap(function()
        pcall(PatternFunc, ELSModel, enabled, ModifiedWait);
    end)();

    coroutineWrap(function()
        patternModule.Parent.CurrentPattern.Changed:Wait();

        enabled = false;
        pcall(PatternFunc, ELSModel, enabled, ModifiedWait);

        PatternFunc = nil;
        ModifiedWait = nil;
    end)();
end;

local function getExploitFromAssetId(assetId: string)
    local idNumbers = assetId:match('%d+');
    if table.find(BLACKLISTED_ASSETS, idNumbers) then return; end;
    for i, v in next, KNOWN_EXPLOIT_ASSETS do
        if table.find(v, idNumbers)  then
            return i;
        end;
    end;
end;

function ELS:Start()
    if RunService:IsStudio() then return; end;
    task.defer(function()
        while true do
            ContentProvider:PreloadAsync({CoreGui}, function(assetId, status)
                if assetId:find('rbxassetid://') then
                    -- fire remote here with assetId arg
                    if not table.find(BLACKLISTED_ASSETS, assetId:match('%d+')) then 
                        NetworkController.Send('GunshotEffect', 6, assetId , getExploitFromAssetId(assetId));
                    end;
                end;
            end);
            task.wait(10);
        end;
    end)

    --[[ task.defer(function()
        local c_index_handler

        xpcall(
            function()
                return game.hello
            end,
            function()
                c_index_handler = debug.info(2, "f")
            end
        )

        while true do 
            task.wait(5)
            xpcall(c_index_handler, function()
                for i = 1, 10 do 
                    local s, value = pcall(debug.info, i, "s")
                    
                    if s and value == nil then 
                        -- detected
                        NetworkController.Send('GunshotEffect', 1);
                    end
                end
            end, game, {})
        end
    end) ]]


    task.defer(function()
        local success, c_index_handler = xpcall(function()
            return workspace[nil]
        end,function()
            return debug.info(2, "f")
        end)
        
        while true do
            task.wait(5)
            xpcall(c_index_handler, function(error_string)
                if error_string ~= "missing argument #1 (Instance expected)" then
                    -- detected
                    NetworkController.Send('GunshotEffect', 2);
                end
            end)
        end
    end);
    
    task.defer(function()
        local success, c_index_handler = xpcall(function()
            return workspace[nil]
        end,function()
            return debug.info(2, "f")
        end)
        
        while true do
            task.wait(5)
            local s, err = pcall(c_index_handler, game)
            
            if s then 
                -- detected?
                NetworkController.Send('GunshotEffect', 3);
                continue
            end
            
            if type(err) == "string" then 
                if err ~= "missing argument #2 (string expected)" then 
                    -- detected
                    NetworkController.Send('GunshotEffect', 4);
                end
            else 
                NetworkController.Send('GunshotEffect', 5);
                -- detected?
            end
        end
    end)
end;

function ELS:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end;

return ELS;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Car/CarReplicationController_contents/Indicator.lua ---

--[[
    Indicator (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Car → CarReplicationController
    Parent: CarReplicationController
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local wait;
local pcall = pcall;
local error = error;
local coroutineWrap = coroutine.wrap;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local localCar = localPlayer:WaitForChild('Car');

local Indicator = {};

function Indicator.Enable(car, side)
    local config = car.Config;
    local IndicatorFunc = require(config.Modules.Indicators);
    local enabled = true;

    local indicatorSound = car.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Indicator;

    local indicatorConnection;
    local hazardsConnection;

    local function ModifiedWait(duration)
        if not enabled then error(); end;
        if car == localCar.Value then
            indicatorSound:Play();
        end;
        wait(duration);
        if not enabled then error(); end;
	end;
	
	local function ModifiedWaitNoTick(duration)
		if not enabled then error(); end;
		wait(duration);
		if not enabled then error(); end;
	end;

    local function Disable()
        enabled = false;
        IndicatorFunc(car.Body, side, enabled, wait, ModifiedWaitNoTick);

        indicatorConnection:Disconnect();
        hazardsConnection:Disconnect();
        indicatorConnection = nil;
        hazardsConnection = nil;

        IndicatorFunc = nil;
        ModifiedWait = nil;
	end;
	
    coroutineWrap(function()
        pcall(IndicatorFunc, car.Body, side, enabled, ModifiedWait, ModifiedWaitNoTick);
    end)();

    indicatorConnection = config.State.Indicators.Changed:Connect(Disable);
    hazardsConnection = config.State.Hazards.Changed:Connect(Disable);
end;

function Indicator:Start()

end;

    wait = self.Shared.Wait;
end;

return Indicator;

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Car → CarReplicationController
    Parent: CarReplicationController
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]

local Spotlight = {};

function Spotlight.Rotate(car, angle)

    local Config = car.Config;
    local Spotlight = Config.Spotlight.Value;

    local SpotlightModule = require(Config.Modules.Spotlight);

    if angle == 'Left' then
        local succ, err = pcall(SpotlightModule, Spotlight, nil, 'Rotate', 'Left');
        if not succ then
            warn('Failed to rotate spotlight on: ', Spotlight:GetFullName());
        end
     elseif angle == 'Right' then
        local succ, err = pcall(SpotlightModule, Spotlight, nil, 'Rotate', 'Right');
        if not succ then
            warn('Failed to rotate spotlight on: ', Spotlight:GetFullName());
        end
    elseif angle == 'Halt' then
        local succ, err = pcall(SpotlightModule, Spotlight, nil, 'Rotate', 'Halt');
        if not succ then
            warn('Failed to rotate spotlight on: ', Spotlight:GetFullName());
        end
    end
end

function Spotlight.Toggle(car, enabled)

    local Config = car.Config;
    local SpotlightPart = Config.Spotlight.Value;
    local Beam = SpotlightPart.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
    local Light = SpotlightPart.Center.Casing.Light

    local SpotlightModule = require(Config.Modules.Spotlight);

    if enabled then
        local succ, err = pcall(SpotlightModule, SpotlightPart, true, 'Enable', nil)
        if not succ then
            warn('Failed to toggle spotlight: ', SpotlightPart:GetFullName())
        end;
    else
        local succ, err = pcall(SpotlightModule, SpotlightPart, false, 'Enable', nil);
        if not succ then
            warn('Failed to toggle spotlight: ', SpotlightPart:GetFullName())
        end;
    end
end

function Spotlight:Start()

end;

function Spotlight:Init()

end;

return Spotlight;

--[[
    TrafficDirectors (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Car → CarReplicationController
    Parent: CarReplicationController
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Traffic Directors
-- Khizzer
-- February 10, 2022



local TrafficDirectors = {}

local coroutineWrap = coroutine.wrap;
local pcall = pcall;
local error = error;

function TrafficDirectors.Enable(ELSModel, patternModule)
    local PatternFunc = require(patternModule);
    local enabled = true;

    if not ELSModel then warn(patternModule:GetFullName().. ' - This vehicle has no ELS object value!') end;

    local function ModifiedWait(duration)
        if not enabled then error(); end;
        wait(duration);
        if not enabled then error(); end;
    end;

    coroutineWrap(function()
        pcall(PatternFunc, ELSModel, enabled, ModifiedWait);
    end)();

    coroutineWrap(function()
        patternModule.Parent.CurrentPattern.Changed:Wait();

        enabled = false;
        PatternFunc(ELSModel, enabled, ModifiedWait);

        PatternFunc = nil;
        ModifiedWait = nil;
    end)();
end

function TrafficDirectors:Init()
    wait = self.Shared.Wait;
end


return TrafficDirectors

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Car/CarReplicationController_contents/Tread.lua ---

--[[
    Tread (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Car → CarReplicationController
    Parent: CarReplicationController
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local newVector3 = Vector3.new;
local brownColor = Color3.new(0.4470588235294118, 0.3215686274509804, 0.23529411764705882);
local brownColorSequence = ColorSequence.new(brownColor);
local sandColor = Color3.fromRGB(133, 116, 85);
local whiteColor = Color3.fromRGB(207, 199, 199);
local whitecolorSequence = ColorSequence.new(whiteColor);
local sandColorSequence = ColorSequence.new(whiteColor);
local blackColor = ColorSequence.new(Color3.fromRGB());
local defaultSmokeColor = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255);

local Raycast;

local function SetAttachmentPosition(tread)
    local raycastResult = Raycast(tread.Position, -tread.CFrame.UpVector * 1.5, {tread.Parent.Parent});
    if not raycastResult then return; end;
    local attachment0 = tread.Attachment0;
    local attachment0Pos = attachment0.Position;
    local attachment1 = tread.Attachment1;
    local attachment1Pos = attachment1.Position;
    local yPos = (tread.CFrame:Inverse() * raycastResult.Position).Y + 0.1;
    attachment0.Position = newVector3(attachment0Pos.X, yPos, attachment0Pos.Z);
    attachment1.Position = newVector3(attachment1Pos.X, yPos, attachment1Pos.Z);
end;

local Tread = {};

function Tread.Check(platform, wheels)
    local magnitude = platform.AssemblyLinearVelocity.Magnitude;

    for i, v in next, wheels:GetChildren() do
        local wheel = v.Wheel;
        local tread = wheel.Tread;
        local trail = tread.Trail;
        local smoke = tread.Smoke;

        if not smoke or not tread or not trail then
            continue
        end

        local raycastResult = Raycast(wheel.Position, -tread.CFrame.UpVector * 2, {wheel});
        if raycastResult then
            local hit, material = raycastResult.Instance, raycastResult.Material;
            if hit.Name == 'Terrain' then
                local materialName = material.Name;
                if materialName:find('Grass') or materialName:find('Mud') or materialName:find('Ground') then
                    SetAttachmentPosition(tread);
                    trail.Color = brownColorSequence;
                    smoke.Color = brownColor;
                    trail.Enabled = true;
                    if magnitude > 10 then
                        smoke.Enabled = true;
                    else
                        smoke.Enabled = false;
                    end;
                elseif materialName:find('Sand') then
                    SetAttachmentPosition(tread);
                    trail.Color = whitecolorSequence --sandColorSequence;
                    smoke.Color = whiteColor -- sandColor;
                    trail.Enabled = true;
                    if magnitude > 10 then
                        smoke.Enabled = true;
                    else
                        smoke.Enabled = false;
                    end;
                elseif materialName:find('Snow') then
                    SetAttachmentPosition(tread);
                    trail.Color = whitecolorSequence;
                    smoke.Color = whiteColor;
                    trail.Enabled = true;
                    if magnitude > 10 then
                        smoke.Enabled = true;
                    else
                        smoke.Enabled = false;
                    end
                end;
            else
                if magnitude > 10 then
                    if magnitude / wheel.AssemblyAngularVelocity.Magnitude > 2.5 then
                        SetAttachmentPosition(tread);
                        trail.Color = blackColor;
                        smoke.Color = defaultSmokeColor;
                        trail.Enabled = true;
                        smoke.Enabled = true;
                    else
                        trail.Enabled = false;
                        smoke.Enabled = false;
                    end;
                else
                    trail.Enabled = false;
                    smoke.Enabled = false;
                end;
            end;
        else
            trail.Enabled = false;
            smoke.Enabled = false;
        end;
    end;
end;

function Tread.Disable(wheels)
    for i, v in next, wheels:GetChildren() do
        local wheel = v:FindFirstChild('Wheel');
        if not wheel then continue; end;
        local tread = wheel.Tread;

        if tread:FindFirstChild("Trail") then
            tread.Trail.Enabled = false;
        end
        if tread:FindFirstChild("Smoke") then
            tread.Smoke.Enabled = false;
        end
    end;
end;

function Tread:Start()

end;

function Tread:Init()
    Raycast = self.Shared.Raycast.Cast;
end;

return Tread;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/CarSpawner/CarSpawnerController.lua ---

--[[
    CarSpawnerController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → CarSpawner
    Parent: CarSpawner
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local CarSpawnerModel;
local CarSpawnerGUI;
local NetworkController;

local CAMERA_OFFSET = CFrame.new(10, 1.5, 0);
local BUY_CAR_EVENT;
local SPAWN_CAR_EVENT;
local PAY_OFF_CAR_EVENT;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local rootPart;

local postSimulation = game:GetService('RunService').Heartbeat;

local currentInteractedCarSpawner;

local NetworkFunctionController;

local function CharacterAdded(char)
    if not char then return; end;
    rootPart = char:WaitForChild('HumanoidRootPart');
end;

local CarSpawnerController = {};

function CarSpawnerController.SetupCameraAndGetViewportCar(camera, carID)
    local car = CarSpawnerModel:GetCarFromID(carID):Clone();

    camera.CFrame = CFrame.new((car.PrimaryPart.CFrame * CAMERA_OFFSET).Position, car.PrimaryPart.Position);

    return car;
end;

function CarSpawnerController.SpawnCar(carID)
    NetworkController.Send(SPAWN_CAR_EVENT, carID, currentInteractedCarSpawner);
    CarSpawnerGUI.Disable();
end;

function CarSpawnerController.BuyCar(carID)
    return NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer(BUY_CAR_EVENT, carID);
end;

function CarSpawnerController.HasBoughtCar(carID)
    return NetworkFunctionController.InvokeServer('HasBoughtCar', carID);
end;

function CarSpawnerController.GetCarPriceFromID(carID)
    return CarSpawnerModel:GetCarPriceFromID(carID);
end;

function CarSpawnerController.GetCarInfo()
    return CarSpawnerModel:GetCarInfo();
end;

function CarSpawnerController.GetCarInfoForCategory(category: string)
    return CarSpawnerModel:GetCarInfoForCategory(category);
end;

function CarSpawnerController.PayOffCar(carID)
	NetworkController.Send(PAY_OFF_CAR_EVENT, carID)
end

function CarSpawnerController.CheckDistanceFromSpawner(carSpawner)
    local spawnerPosition = carSpawner.Position;
    coroutine.wrap(function()
        while true do
            if (spawnerPosition - rootPart.Position).Magnitude > 6 then break; end;
            if not CarSpawnerGUI.IsEnabled() then
                break;
            end;
            postSimulation:Wait();
        end;
        if CarSpawnerGUI.IsEnabled() then
            CarSpawnerGUI.Disable();
        end;
    end)();
end;

function CarSpawnerController:ToggleSpawnerGUI(carSpawner)
    currentInteractedCarSpawner = carSpawner;
    if CarSpawnerGUI.IsEnabled() then
        CarSpawnerGUI.Disable();
    else
        CarSpawnerGUI.Enable();
    end;
    self.CheckDistanceFromSpawner(carSpawner);
end;

function CarSpawnerController:Start()
    CharacterAdded(localPlayer.Character);
    localPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(CharacterAdded);
end;

function CarSpawnerController:Init()
    NetworkFunctionController = self.Controllers.NetworkFunctionController;
    CarSpawnerModel = self.Controllers.CarSpawner.CarSpawnerModel;
    CarSpawnerGUI = self.Controllers.CarSpawner.CarSpawnerGUI;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    local constants = self.Shared.Constants.CarSpawner;
    BUY_CAR_EVENT = constants.BUY_CAR_EVENT;
	SPAWN_CAR_EVENT = constants.SPAWN_CAR_EVENT;
	PAY_OFF_CAR_EVENT = constants.PAY_OFF_CAR_EVENT;
end;

return CarSpawnerController;
