--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/CarSpawner/CarSpawnerGUI.lua ---

--[[
    CarSpawnerGUI (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → CarSpawner
    Parent: CarSpawner
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local CarSpawnerController;

local DEFAULT_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 1.5);
local ACTIVE_POSITION = UDim2.fromScale(0.5, 0.5);
local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23);
local HOVER_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 50);
local DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40);
local SELECTED_BTN_COLOR = Color3.fromRGB(79, 121, 159);
local PRICE_PREFIX = '$';

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local carSpawnerGUI = localPlayer.PlayerGui:WaitForChild('CarSpawnerGUI');
local mainFrame = carSpawnerGUI.MainFrame;
local bodyFrame = mainFrame.BodyFrame;

local btnsFrame = bodyFrame.BtnsFrame;
local exitBtn = btnsFrame.ExitBtn;
local buyBtn = btnsFrame.BuyBtn;
local spawnBtn = btnsFrame.SpawnBtn;

local carsListScrollingFrame = bodyFrame.CarsListImage.CarsListScrollingFrame;
local packageListScrollingFrame = bodyFrame.CarsListImage.PackageCarsListScrollingFrame;

local detailsFrame = bodyFrame.DetailsFrame;
local carViewportFrame = detailsFrame.CarViewportFrame;
local nameLabel = detailsFrame.NameLabel;
local priceLabel = detailsFrame.PriceLabel;

local components = carSpawnerGUI.Components;
local carBtnPrefab = components.CarBtn;

local openTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = ACTIVE_POSITION});
local closeTween = TweenService:Create(mainFrame, TWEEN_INFO, {Position = DEFAULT_POSITION});

local selectedBtn;

local buyConnection;
local spawnConnection;

local viewportCamera;
local viewportCarModel;

local function CreateCamera()
    local camera = Instance.new('Camera');
    return camera;
end;

local function UpdateScrollingFrameCanvasSize()
    carsListScrollingFrame.CanvasSize = UDim2.fromOffset(0, (#carsListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() - 1) * 30);
end;

local function UpdatePackageScrollingFrameCanvasSize()
    packageListScrollingFrame.CanvasSize = UDim2.fromOffset(0, (#packageListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() - 1) * 30);
end;

local CarSpawnerGUI = {};

function CarSpawnerGUI.IsEnabled()
    return carSpawnerGUI.Enabled;
end;

function CarSpawnerGUI.Enable()
    viewportCamera = CreateCamera();
    carViewportFrame.CurrentCamera = viewportCamera;
    carsListScrollingFrame.Visible = true;
    packageListScrollingFrame.Visible = false;

    for i, v in next, CarSpawnerController.GetCarInfo() do
        if typeof(i) ~= "string" then
            --If its just a normal model car with no categories
            local carName = v.Name;
            local carID = v.ID;

            local carBtn = carBtnPrefab:Clone();
            carBtn.CarLabel.Text = carName;
            carBtn.Parent = carsListScrollingFrame;

            local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(carBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
            local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(carBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
            local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(carBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

            local function ReloadBuyAndSpawnBtn()
                local hasBoughtCar = CarSpawnerController.HasBoughtCar(carID);
                if hasBoughtCar then
                    spawnBtn.Visible = true;
                    buyBtn.Visible = false;
                else
                    buyBtn.Visible = true;
                    spawnBtn.Visible = false;
                end;
            end;

            carBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                if selectedBtn == carBtn then return; end;
                hoverTween:Play();
            end);

            carBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                if selectedBtn == carBtn then return; end;
                hoverEndTween:Play();
            end);

            carBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                if selectedBtn then
                    TweenService:Create(selectedBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
                end;

                selectedBtn = carBtn;
                selectedTween:Play();

                nameLabel.Text = carName;
                priceLabel.Text = PRICE_PREFIX .. CarSpawnerController.GetCarPriceFromID(carID);

                if viewportCarModel then
                    viewportCarModel:Destroy();
                end;

                viewportCarModel = CarSpawnerController.SetupCameraAndGetViewportCar(viewportCamera, carID);
                viewportCarModel.Parent = carViewportFrame;

                ReloadBuyAndSpawnBtn();

                if buyConnection then
                    buyConnection:Disconnect();
                end;
                if spawnConnection then
                    spawnConnection:Disconnect();
                end;

                buyConnection = buyBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    CarSpawnerController.BuyCar(carID);
                    ReloadBuyAndSpawnBtn();
                end);

                spawnConnection = spawnBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    CarSpawnerController.SpawnCar(carID);
                end);
            end);
        else
            if #CarSpawnerController.GetCarInfoForCategory(i) == 0 then
                continue
            end
            --i is category name/index for the dictionary. v is table containing same as above
            local categoryBtn = carBtnPrefab:Clone();
            categoryBtn.CarLabel.Text = i;
            categoryBtn.Parent = carsListScrollingFrame;

            local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(categoryBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
            local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(categoryBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});

            categoryBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                hoverTween:Play();
            end);

            categoryBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                hoverEndTween:Play();
            end);

            categoryBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
                carsListScrollingFrame.Visible = false;
                packageListScrollingFrame.Visible = true;
                if buyConnection then
                    buyConnection:Disconnect();
                    buyConnection = nil;
                end
                if spawnConnection then
                    spawnConnection:Disconnect();
                    spawnConnection = nil;
                end
                local backBtn = carBtnPrefab:Clone();
                backBtn.CarLabel.Text = 'Back';
                backBtn.Parent = packageListScrollingFrame;

                backBtn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
                    for _,v3 in next, packageListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
                        if v3:IsA('ImageButton') then
                            v3:Destroy();
                        end
                    end
                    carsListScrollingFrame.Visible = true;
                    packageListScrollingFrame.Visible = false;
                end)

                for i2, v2 in next, CarSpawnerController.GetCarInfoForCategory(i) do
                    local carName = v2.Name;
                    local carID = v2.ID;

                    local carBtn = carBtnPrefab:Clone();
                    carBtn.CarLabel.Text = carName;
                    carBtn.Parent = packageListScrollingFrame;

                    local hoverTween = TweenService:Create(carBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = HOVER_BTN_COLOR});
                    local hoverEndTween = TweenService:Create(carBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR});
                    local selectedTween = TweenService:Create(carBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = SELECTED_BTN_COLOR});

                    local function ReloadBuyAndSpawnBtn()
                        local hasBoughtCar = CarSpawnerController.HasBoughtCar(carID);
                        if hasBoughtCar then
                            spawnBtn.Visible = true;
                            buyBtn.Visible = false;
                        else
                            buyBtn.Visible = true;
                            spawnBtn.Visible = false;
                        end;
                    end;

                    carBtn.MouseEnter:Connect(function()
                        if selectedBtn == carBtn then return; end;
                        hoverTween:Play();
                    end);

                    carBtn.MouseLeave:Connect(function()
                        if selectedBtn == carBtn then return; end;
                        hoverEndTween:Play();
                    end);

                    carBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                        if selectedBtn then
                            TweenService:Create(selectedBtn, TWEEN_INFO, {ImageColor3 = DEFAULT_BTN_COLOR}):Play();
                        end;

                        selectedBtn = carBtn;
                        selectedTween:Play();

                        nameLabel.Text = carName;
                        priceLabel.Text = PRICE_PREFIX .. CarSpawnerController.GetCarPriceFromID(carID);

                        if viewportCarModel then
                            viewportCarModel:Destroy();
                        end;

                        viewportCarModel = CarSpawnerController.SetupCameraAndGetViewportCar(viewportCamera, carID);
                        viewportCarModel.Parent = carViewportFrame;

                        ReloadBuyAndSpawnBtn();

                        if buyConnection then
                            buyConnection:Disconnect();
                        end;
                        if spawnConnection then
                            spawnConnection:Disconnect();
                        end;

                        buyConnection = buyBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                            local boughtCar = CarSpawnerController.BuyCar(carID); --Changed to network function, returns true if bought
                            if boughtCar == true then
                                ReloadBuyAndSpawnBtn();
                            end;
                        end);

                        spawnConnection = spawnBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                            CarSpawnerController.SpawnCar(carID);
                            for _,v3 in next, packageListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
                                if v3:IsA('ImageButton') then
                                    v3:Destroy();
                                end
                            end
                        end);
                    end);
                end
                UpdatePackageScrollingFrameCanvasSize();
            end)
        end;
    end;

    UpdateScrollingFrameCanvasSize();

    carSpawnerGUI.Enabled = true;
    openTween:Play();
end;

function CarSpawnerGUI.Disable()
    closeTween:Play();
    closeTween.Completed:Wait();
    carSpawnerGUI.Enabled = false;

    selectedBtn = nil;
    nameLabel.Text = '';
    priceLabel.Text = '';
    spawnBtn.Visible = false;
    buyBtn.Visible = false;
    carViewportFrame.CurrentCamera = nil;
    if viewportCamera then
        viewportCamera:Destroy();
    end;
    if viewportCarModel then
        viewportCarModel:Destroy();
    end;
    if buyConnection then
        buyConnection:Disconnect();
        buyConnection = nil;
    end;
    if spawnConnection then
        spawnConnection:Disconnect();
        spawnConnection = nil;
    end;

    for i, v in next, carsListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
            v:Destroy();
        end;
    end;

    for i,v in next, packageListScrollingFrame:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('ImageButton') then
            v:Destroy();
        end;
    end;
end;

function CarSpawnerGUI:Start()
    mainFrame.Position = DEFAULT_POSITION;

    exitBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(self.Disable);
end;

function CarSpawnerGUI:Init()
    CarSpawnerController = self.Controllers.CarSpawner.CarSpawnerController;
end;

return CarSpawnerGUI;



================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/CarSpawner/CarSpawnerModel.lua ---

--[[
    CarSpawnerModel (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → CarSpawner
    Parent: CarSpawner
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local cars = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage'):WaitForChild('Cars');

local DeveloperCheck;

local CarSpawnerModel = {};

function CarSpawnerModel.GetCarsFolderForLocalPlayer()
    local jobName = localPlayer:GetAttribute('CurrentJob');
    local division = localPlayer:GetAttribute('Division');
    local folder = (jobName and cars:FindFirstChild(jobName)) or (division and cars:FindFirstChild(division)) or cars:FindFirstChild(localPlayer.Team.Name)
    if folder:GetAttribute("Redirect") then
        local newFolder = cars:FindFirstChild(folder:GetAttribute("Redirect"))
        if not newFolder then
            warn(`Invalid redirect folder \`${folder:GetAttribute("Redirect")}\` for {folder.Name}`)
            return folder
        end
        return newFolder
    end
    return folder

    -- return (CIVILIAN_REDIRECT_TEAMS[localPlayer.Team.Name] == true and cars['Civilian']) or ;
end;

function CarSpawnerModel:GetCarFromID(carID)
    local carsFolder = self.GetCarsFolderForLocalPlayer();
    for i, v in next, carsFolder:GetChildren() do
        if v:IsA('Model') then
            local spawnerSettings = v.Config.SpawnerSettings;
            if spawnerSettings.ID.Value == carID then
                return v;
            end;
        else
            for i2, v2 in next, v:GetChildren() do
                local spawnerSettings = v2.Config.SpawnerSettings;
                if spawnerSettings.ID.Value == carID then
                    return v2;
                end;
            end
        end;
    end;
end;

function CarSpawnerModel:GetCarPriceFromID(carID)
    return self:GetCarFromID(carID).Config.SpawnerSettings.Price.Value;
end;

function CarSpawnerModel:GetCarInfo()
    local info = {};

    local proxySortedKeys = {};

    local CarsFolderForLocalPlayer = {};

    --This sorts out the cars in order of price
    do
        for _,v in next, self.GetCarsFolderForLocalPlayer():GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('Model') then
                table.insert(proxySortedKeys, v);
            end;
        end;

        table.sort(proxySortedKeys, function(a, b)
            local aPrice = a.Config.SpawnerSettings.Price.Value;
            local bPrice = b.Config.SpawnerSettings.Price.Value;

            if aPrice == bPrice then
                return a.Name < b.Name;
            end;

            return a.Config.SpawnerSettings.Price.Value < b.Config.SpawnerSettings.Price.Value;
        end);
    end;

    --Add the cars with different package selections to the bottom of the list (they are all police so it doesnt matter about price)
    do
        --For each car in the sorted keys, add it to the CarsFolderForLocalPlayer table
        for _,v in next, proxySortedKeys do
            table.insert(CarsFolderForLocalPlayer, v);
        end;

        for _,v in next, self.GetCarsFolderForLocalPlayer():GetChildren() do
            if v:IsA('Folder') then
                table.insert(CarsFolderForLocalPlayer, v);
            end;
        end;
    end

    for i, v in next, CarsFolderForLocalPlayer do
        if v:IsA('Model') then
            local spawnerSettings = v.Config.SpawnerSettings;
            local groupID = spawnerSettings:FindFirstChild('GroupID');
            local minRank = groupID and spawnerSettings:FindFirstChild('MinRank');
            local condition = spawnerSettings:FindFirstChild('Condition');
            local conditionFunc = if condition then require(condition) else function() return false end;
            if (not minRank) or DeveloperCheck(localPlayer) or (localPlayer:GetRankInGroup(groupID.Value) >= minRank.Value) or conditionFunc(localPlayer) then
                table.insert(info, {
                    Name = v.Name,
                    ID = spawnerSettings.ID.Value
                });
            end;
        elseif v:IsA('Folder') then
            info[v.Name] = {};
            local carTable = info[v.Name];
            for _,car in next, v:GetChildren() do
                local spawnerSettings = car.Config.SpawnerSettings;
                local groupID = spawnerSettings:FindFirstChild('GroupID');
                local minRank = groupID and spawnerSettings:FindFirstChild('MinRank');
                local condition = spawnerSettings:FindFirstChild('Condition');
                local conditionFunc = if condition then require(condition) else function() return false end;
				if (not minRank) or DeveloperCheck(localPlayer) or (localPlayer:GetRankInGroup(groupID.Value) >= minRank.Value) or conditionFunc(localPlayer) then
                    table.insert(carTable, {
                        Name = car.Name,
                        ID = spawnerSettings.ID.Value
                    });
                end;
            end;
        end;
    end;
    return info;
end;

function CarSpawnerModel:GetCarInfoForCategory(category: string)
    local info = {};
    for i, v in next, self.GetCarsFolderForLocalPlayer()[category]:GetChildren() do
        local spawnerSettings = v.Config.SpawnerSettings;
        local groupID = spawnerSettings:FindFirstChild('GroupID');
        local minRank = groupID and spawnerSettings:FindFirstChild('MinRank');
        local condition = spawnerSettings:FindFirstChild('Condition');
        local conditionFunc = if condition then require(condition) else function() return false end;
		if (not minRank) or DeveloperCheck(localPlayer) or (localPlayer:GetRankInGroup(groupID.Value) >= minRank.Value) or conditionFunc(localPlayer) then
            table.insert(info, {
                Name = v.Name,
                ID = spawnerSettings.ID.Value
            });
        end
    end;
    return info;
end

function CarSpawnerModel:Start()

end;

function CarSpawnerModel:Init()
    DeveloperCheck = self.Shared.DeveloperCheck;
end;

return CarSpawnerModel;

-- Animation Controller
-- Khizzer
-- July 23, 2022



local AnimationController = {}

local NetworkController;

local localPLayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local playerScripts = localPLayer:WaitForChild('PlayerScripts');
local storage = playerScripts:WaitForChild('Storage');
local animationStorage = storage:WaitForChild('Animations');
local SUSPECT_CUFF_ANIMATION = animationStorage:WaitForChild('SuspectCuff');
local OFFICER_CUFF_ANIMATION = animationStorage:WaitForChild('OfficerCuff');

local suspectCuffTrack;
local officerCuffTrack;

function AnimationController:CharacterAdded(char: Model)
    if not char then return; end;
    local humanoid: Humanoid = char:WaitForChild('Humanoid');
    for _, animation in {suspectCuffTrack, officerCuffTrack} do
        if animation then
            animation:Destroy();
        end;
    end;

    local animator = humanoid:WaitForChild('Animator');

    suspectCuffTrack = animator:LoadAnimation(SUSPECT_CUFF_ANIMATION);
    officerCuffTrack = animator:LoadAnimation(OFFICER_CUFF_ANIMATION);
end;

function AnimationController:Start()
    NetworkController.Connect('SuspectCuffAnimation', function(play: boolean)
        if play then
            suspectCuffTrack:Play();
        else
            suspectCuffTrack:Stop();
        end;
    end)

    NetworkController.Connect('OfficerCuffAnimation', function(play: boolean)
        if play then
            officerCuffTrack:Play();
        else
            officerCuffTrack:Stop();
        end;
    end)
end;

function AnimationController:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end;


return AnimationController

--[[
    BreathController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Character
    Parent: Character
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
-- Breath Controller
-- Khizzer
-- March 14, 2024

local TERRAIN_VOXEL_SIZE = 4;
local WATER_MATERIAL = Enum.Material.Water;

local BottomRightGUI;

local function IsInWater(pos: Vector3)
	local voxelPos = workspace.Terrain:WorldToCell(pos);
    
	local voxelRegion = Region3.new(voxelPos * TERRAIN_VOXEL_SIZE, (voxelPos + Vector3.one) * TERRAIN_VOXEL_SIZE);
	local materials = workspace.Terrain:ReadVoxels(voxelRegion, TERRAIN_VOXEL_SIZE);
	local voxelMaterial = materials[1][1][1];

	return voxelMaterial == WATER_MATERIAL;
end

local head: Part?;

local BreathController = {}

local NetworkController;

local oxygen = 125;
local MAX_OXYGEN = 125;

local lastInWater = tick();

function BreathController:Start()

end

function BreathController:CharacterAdded(_char)
    head = _char:WaitForChild('Head');

    oxygen = MAX_OXYGEN;

    while head:IsDescendantOf(workspace) do
        if IsInWater(head.Position + Vector3.yAxis) then
            oxygen = math.max(oxygen - 1, 0);
            lastInWater = tick(); -- Reset the timer when the player is in water
        else
            if tick() - lastInWater > 2 then
                oxygen = math.min(oxygen + 1, MAX_OXYGEN);
            end
        end

        BottomRightGUI:SetCharacterBar('Oxygen', oxygen, MAX_OXYGEN);
        if oxygen <= 0 then
            NetworkController.Send('Drown');
        end
        task.wait(0.3);
    end;
end

function BreathController:Init()
    BottomRightGUI = self.Controllers.UI.BottomRightGUI;
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end

return BreathController

--[[local function WaitForTag(instance, tagName)
    if CollectionService:HasTag(instance, tagName) then
        return {Event = {Wait = function() end}};
    end;

    local bindableEvent = Instance.new('BindableEvent');

local CharacterController = {};

local mostRecentTrack;

local function CharacterAdded(char)
    if not char then return; end;

    if mostRecentTrack then
        mostRecentTrack:Destroy();
        mostRecentTrack = nil;
    end

    local humanoid: Humanoid = char:WaitForChild('Humanoid');
    --local rootPart = char:WaitForChild('HumanoidRootPart');

    EnableFirstPersonTransparency(char:WaitForChild('Right Arm'));
    EnableFirstPersonTransparency(char:WaitForChild('Left Arm'));

    humanoid:GetPropertyChangedSignal('SeatPart'):Connect(function()
        local seat = humanoid.SeatPart;

        if seat then
            local anim = seat:FindFirstChildOfClass('Animation');
            if anim then
                local animator: Animator = humanoid.Animator;
                mostRecentTrack = animator:LoadAnimation(anim);
                mostRecentTrack:Play();
            end
        else
            if mostRecentTrack then
                mostRecentTrack:Stop();
                mostRecentTrack:Destroy();
                mostRecentTrack = nil;
            end;
        end
    end)

    humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
        humanoid:UnequipTools();
    end);

    local rootPart = char:WaitForChild('HumanoidRootPart');
    local ringtone = rootPart:WaitForChild('PhoneRingtone');
    ringtone.Muffle:Destroy();

    --[[coroutine.wrap(function()
        WaitForTag(rootPart, 'HumanoidRootPart').Event:Wait();
        CollectionService:RemoveTag(rootPart, 'HumanoidRootPart');
    end)();]]
end;

function CharacterController:Start()
    CharacterAdded(localPlayer.Character);
    localPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(CharacterAdded);
end;

function CharacterController:Init()
	--CarController = self.Controllers.Car.CarController;
end;

return CharacterController;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Character/CombatController.lua ---

--[[
    CombatController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Character
    Parent: Character
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local CombatController = {};
local NetworkController;
local CooldownTime = 0;

local MaxCombatTime = 60;

function CombatController:GetResetTime()
	return CooldownTime, MaxCombatTime;
end;

function CombatController:Start()
	task.spawn(function()
		while task.wait(1) do
			if CooldownTime ~= 0 then
				CooldownTime = CooldownTime - 1
			end
		end
	end)

	NetworkController.Connect('CombatResetSys', function(timing)
		if tonumber(timing) ~= nil then
			CooldownTime = tonumber(timing)
			MaxCombatTime = tonumber(timing)
		end
	end)
end;

function CombatController:Init()
	NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end;

return CombatController;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Character/FallDamageController.lua ---

--[[
    FallDamageController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Character
    Parent: Character
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local NetworkController;

local FREEFALL_STATE = Enum.HumanoidStateType.Freefall;
local LANDED_STATE = Enum.HumanoidStateType.Landed;
local FALL_DAMAGE_EVENT = 'FallDamage';

local fallStartHeight;

local FallDamageController = {};

local function Setup(char)
    if not char then return; end;

    local humanoid = char:WaitForChild('Humanoid');
    local rootPart = char:WaitForChild('HumanoidRootPart');

    fallStartHeight = nil;

    humanoid.StateChanged:Connect(function(oldState, newState)
        if newState == FREEFALL_STATE then
            fallStartHeight = rootPart.Position.Y;
        elseif oldState == FREEFALL_STATE and newState == LANDED_STATE and fallStartHeight then
            local fallHeight = fallStartHeight - rootPart.Position.Y;
            if fallHeight >= 15 then
                NetworkController.Send(FALL_DAMAGE_EVENT, 5 * (fallHeight / 10));
            end;
        end;
    end);
end;

function FallDamageController:Start()
    local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

    Setup(localPlayer.Character);
    localPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(Setup);
end;

function FallDamageController:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
end;

return FallDamageController;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Character/LookController.lua ---

--[[
    LookController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Character
    Parent: Character
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local StarterGui = game:GetService("StarterGui")
local TweenService = game:GetService('TweenService');

local MOTOR6D_NAME = 'Motor6D';
local LEFT_SHOULDER_NAME = 'Left Shoulder';
local RIGHT_SHOULDER_NAME = 'Right Shoulder';
local VEHICLE_SEAT_NAME = 'VehicleSeat';
local TWEEN_INFO = TweenInfo.new(0.23, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out);
local TWEEN_INFO_2 = TweenInfo.new(0.3, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.Out);
local WAIT_TIME = 0.25;

local wait;
local anglesCFrame = CFrame.Angles;
local mathAsin = math.asin;
local mathClamp = math.clamp;
local findFirstChild = workspace.FindFirstChild;
local toObjectSpace = CFrame.new().ToObjectSpace;
local isA = workspace.IsA;
local tweenCreate = TweenService.Create;

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;
local mouse = localPlayer:GetMouse();

local lookEvent;

local char;
local rootPart;
local humanoid;
local neck;
local leftShoulder;
local rightShoulder;

local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera;

local oldNeckC0;
local oldLeftShoulderC0;
local oldRightShoulderC0;

local lookVectorX;
local lastLookVectorX;
local lastSentLookVectorX;

local lookVectorY;
local lastLookVectorY;
local lastSentLookVectorY;

local mouseControl = false;

local function SetCharacterLook(other, neck, leftShoulder, rightShoulder, lookVectorX, lookVectorY)
    tweenCreate(TweenService, neck, other and TWEEN_INFO_2 or TWEEN_INFO, {C0 = oldNeckC0 * anglesCFrame(-mathAsin(mathClamp(lookVectorY, -0.4, 0.4)), 0, -mathAsin(mathClamp(lookVectorX, -0.7, 0.7)))}):Play();
    if char:FindFirstChild('Attack Line') then
        lookVectorY = mathClamp(lookVectorY, -0.45, 0.45);
    else
        lookVectorY = mathClamp(lookVectorY, -0.35, 0.35);
    end;
    tweenCreate(TweenService, leftShoulder, other and TWEEN_INFO_2 or TWEEN_INFO, {C0 = oldLeftShoulderC0 * anglesCFrame(0, 0, -lookVectorY)}):Play();
    tweenCreate(TweenService, rightShoulder, other and TWEEN_INFO_2 or TWEEN_INFO, {C0 = oldRightShoulderC0 * anglesCFrame(0, 0, lookVectorY)}):Play();
end;

local function PostSimulation()
    debug.profilebegin('LocalPlayerHeadDirection');
    local cameraSubject = camera.CameraSubject;

    if (cameraSubject == humanoid) or (isA(cameraSubject, VEHICLE_SEAT_NAME)) then
        local cameraDirection;
        if mouseControl then
            cameraDirection = toObjectSpace(rootPart.CFrame, mouse.Hit).LookVector;
        else
            cameraDirection = toObjectSpace(rootPart.CFrame, camera.CFrame).LookVector;
        end;

        lookVectorX = cameraDirection.X;
        lookVectorY = cameraDirection.Y;

        if (lastLookVectorX ~= lookVectorX) or (lastLookVectorY ~= lookVectorY) then
            lastLookVectorX = lookVectorX;
            lastLookVectorY = lookVectorY;
            SetCharacterLook(false, neck, leftShoulder, rightShoulder, lookVectorX, lookVectorY);
        end;
    end;
    debug.profileend();
end;

local LookController = {};

function LookController:CharacterAdded(character)
	if not character then return; end;

	char = character;
	rootPart = char:WaitForChild('HumanoidRootPart');
	humanoid = char:WaitForChild('Humanoid');
    local torso = char:WaitForChild('Torso');
	neck = torso:FindFirstChild('Neck');
	leftShoulder = char:FindFirstChild('Left Shoulder', true);
	rightShoulder = char:FindFirstChild('Right Shoulder', true);

	oldNeckC0 = neck.C0;
	oldLeftShoulderC0 = leftShoulder.C0;
	oldRightShoulderC0 = rightShoulder.C0;
end;

function LookController.SetMouseControl(enabled)
    mouseControl = enabled;
end;

function LookController:Start()
    repeat task.wait() until rootPart;

	game:GetService('RunService').Heartbeat:Connect(PostSimulation);

    lookEvent:Connect(function(char, lookVectorX, lookVectorY)
        local plrTorso = char:FindFirstChild('Torso');
        if not plrTorso then return; end;
        local plrNeck = plrTorso:FindFirstChild('Neck');
        if plrNeck and isA(plrNeck, MOTOR6D_NAME) then
            local plrLeftShoulder = findFirstChild(char, LEFT_SHOULDER_NAME, true);
            local plrRightShoulder = findFirstChild(char, RIGHT_SHOULDER_NAME, true);
            if plrLeftShoulder and plrRightShoulder then
                SetCharacterLook(true, plrNeck, plrLeftShoulder, plrRightShoulder, lookVectorX, lookVectorY);
            end;
        end;
    end);

    while true do
        -- If in freecam, leave look as is
        if StarterGui:GetCoreGuiEnabled(Enum.CoreGuiType.Health) == false then
            task.wait(WAIT_TIME)
            continue
        end

        local cameraSubject = camera.CameraSubject;

        if (cameraSubject == humanoid) or (isA(cameraSubject, VEHICLE_SEAT_NAME)) then
            if (lookVectorX ~= lastSentLookVectorX) or (lookVectorY ~= lastSentLookVectorY) then
                lookEvent:Fire(lookVectorX, lookVectorY)
                --NetworkController.Send(LOOK_EVENT, lookVectorX, lookVectorY);
                lastSentLookVectorX = lookVectorX;
                lastSentLookVectorY = lookVectorY;
            end;
        end;

        task.wait(WAIT_TIME);
    end;
end;

function LookController:Init()
    lookEvent = self.Services.LookService.Look;
end;

return LookController;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Character/RagdollController.lua ---

--[[
    RagdollController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Character
    Parent: Character
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local RagdollController = {};
local RunService = game:GetService('RunService')

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local DownedGUI;

local attachments = {
    ['Neck'] = {'NeckAttachment', 'NeckAttachment2'},
    ['Right Shoulder'] = {'RightCollarAttachment', 'RightShoulderAttachment'},
    ['Left Shoulder'] = {'LeftCollarAttachment', 'LeftShoulderAttachment'},
    ['Right Hip'] = {'RightHipAttachment', 'RightLegAttachment'},
    ['Left Hip'] = {'LeftHipAttachment', 'LeftLegAttachment'}
};

local NetworkController;

local ballConstraints = {};

local newInstance = Instance.new;

local function CreateAttachment(name, parent, position)
    local attachment = newInstance('Attachment');
    attachment.Name = name;
    attachment.Position = position;
    attachment.Parent = parent;
    return attachment;
end;

local healthChanged;
local died;

local runServiceConnection;

local ragdollFunction;

function RagdollController:CharacterAdded(char)
    if not char then return; end;

    local humanoid: Humanoid = char:WaitForChild('Humanoid');
    local torso = char:WaitForChild('Torso');

    if healthChanged then
        healthChanged:Disconnect();
        healthChanged = nil;
    end;

    if runServiceConnection then
        runServiceConnection:Disconnect();
        runServiceConnection = nil;
    end;

    local function Ragdoll(state: boolean)
        if state == true then
            task.defer(function()
                runServiceConnection = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
                    if humanoid:GetState() ~= Enum.HumanoidStateType.Physics then
                        humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Physics);
                    end;
                end);
            end)
        else
            if runServiceConnection then
                runServiceConnection:Disconnect();
                runServiceConnection = nil;
                humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.FallingDown);
            end;
        end;
    end;

    ragdollFunction = Ragdoll;

    humanoid.BreakJointsOnDeath = false;

    healthChanged = humanoid.HealthChanged:Connect(function(health)
        if health <= 1 then
            if not char.Parent then return; end;
            Ragdoll(true);
        elseif health > 1 then
            if not char.Parent then return; end;
            Ragdoll(false);
        end;
    end);

    died = humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
        if not char.Parent then return; end;
        task.spawn(DownedGUI.Enable, DownedGUI);
        died:Disconnect();
        died = nil;
        if runServiceConnection then
            runServiceConnection:Disconnect();
            runServiceConnection = nil;
        end;
    end);
end;

function RagdollController:Start()
    NetworkController.Connect('DISABLE_RAGDOLL', function()
        if not ragdollFunction then return; end;
        ragdollFunction(false);
    end);
end;

function RagdollController:Init()
    NetworkController = self.Controllers.NetworkController;
    DownedGUI = self.Controllers.UI.DownedGUI;
end;

return RagdollController;

--- SCRIPT PATH: StarterPlayer/StarterPlayerScripts/vClient/Controllers/Character/ResetController.lua ---

--[[
    ResetController (ModuleScript)
    Path: StarterPlayer → StarterPlayerScripts → vClient → Controllers → Character
    Parent: Character
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:56
]]
local StarterGui = game:GetService('StarterGui');

local localPlayer = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer;

local CombatController;

local resetBindableEvent = Instance.new('BindableEvent');
local ResetController = {};

function ResetController:Start()
    resetBindableEvent.Event:Connect(function()
		if CombatController:GetResetTime() > 0 then
			self.Controllers.UI.Notification.new('In Combat', 'You are in combat! Please wait '..tostring(CombatController:GetResetTime() or 0)..' seconds to be able to reset.', nil, 'Red')
		elseif localPlayer:GetAttribute('HandcuffedBy') then
			self.Controllers.UI.Notification.new('Detained', 'You cannot reset while detained.', nil, 'Red')
		elseif localPlayer.Team.Name == "Prisoner" then
			-- TODO: Let prisoners reset if they've escaped?
			self.Controllers.UI.Notification.new('Imprisoned', 'You cannot reset while in prison.', nil, 'Black')
		else
			self.Controllers.NetworkController.Send('Reset');
		end
	end);

	while true do
        local suc = pcall(function()
            StarterGui:SetCore('ResetButtonCallback', resetBindableEvent);
        end);
        if suc then break; end;
        task.wait();
    end;
end;

function ResetController:Init()
	CombatController = self.Controllers.Character.CombatController;
end;

return ResetController;
